{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1}
guṇatrayavibhedena mūrtitrayam upaiyuṣe | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 1.1]
trayībhuve trinetrāya trilokīpataye namaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 1.2]
sarasvatyai namo yasyāḥ prasādāt puṇyakarmabhiḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 2.1]
buddhidarpaṇasaṃkrāntaṃ jagadadhyakṣam īkṣyate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 2.2]
brahmadakṣāśvideveśabharadvājapunarvasuhutāśaveśacarakaprabhṛtibhyo namo namaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 3]
pātañjalamahābhāṣyacarakapratisaṃskṛtaiḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 4.1]
manovākkāyadoṣāṇāṃ hartre 'hipataye namaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 4.2]
naradattagurūddiṣṭacarakārthānugāminī | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 5.1]
kriyate cakradattena ṭīkāyurvedadīpikā | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 5.2]
sabhyāḥ sadguruvāksudhāsrutiparisphītaśrutīn asmi vo nālaṃ toṣayituṃ payodapayasā nāmbhonidhis tṛpyati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 6.1]
vyākhyābhāsarasaprakāśanam idaṃ tv asmin yadi prāpyate kvāpi kvāpi kaṇo guṇasya tadasau karṇe kṣaṇaṃ dhīyatām | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 6.2]
iha hi dharmārthakāmamokṣaparipanthirogopaśamāya brahmaprabhṛtibhiḥ praṇītāyurvedatantreṣvativistaratvena samprati vartamānālpāyurmedhasāṃ puruṣāṇāṃ na samyagarthādhigamaḥ tadanadhigamācca tadvihitārthānāmananuṣṭhāne tathaivopaplavo rujāmiti manvānaḥ paramakāruṇiko 'trabhavān agniveśo'lpāyurmedhasāmapi suropalambhārthaṃ nātisaṃkṣepavistaraṃ kāyacikitsāpradhānam āyurvedatantraṃ praṇetum ārabdhavān | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 7]
tasmiṃśca ślokanidānavimānaśārīrendriyacikitsitakalpasiddhisthānātmake 'bhidhātavye nikhilatantrapradhānārthābhidhāya | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 8]
ktā ityādivākyābhidhāyakena darśitaṃ mantavyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 9]
nanu prayojanābhidhānaṃ śāstrapravṛttyarthamiti yaduktaṃ tanna yuktaṃ yato na prayojanābhidhānamātreṇa prayojanavattāvadhāraṇaṃ vipralambhakasaṃsāramocanapratipādakādiśāstreṣu prayojanābhidhāne'pi niṣprayojanatvadarśanāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 10]
atha manyase āptaprayojanābhidhānametadato'tra yathārthatvaṃ nanu bho kathamayaṃ prayojanābhidhāyī āptaḥ tadabhihitaśāstrasya yathārthatvāditi cet hanta na yāvacchāstrasya prayojanavattāvadhāraṇaṃ na tāvacchāstrapravṛttiḥ na yāvacchāstrapravṛttir na tāvacchāstrasya yathārthatvāvadhāraṇaṃ na yāvacchāstrasya yathārthatvāvadhāraṇaṃ na tāvacchāstrasya karturāptatvamavadhāryate āptatvānavadhṛtau ca kutas tadabhihitaprayojanavattāvadhāraṇam iti cakrakamāpadyate atha manyase mā bhavatu prayojanavattāvadhāraṇam artharūpaprayojanavattāsaṃdeha eva pravartako bhaviṣyati kṛṣyādāv api hi pravṛttir arthasaṃdehādeva na hi tatra kṛṣīvalānāṃ phalalābhāvadhāraṇaṃ vidyate antarāvagrahāderapisaṃbhāvyamānatvāt nanvevamasatyapi prayojanābhidhāne saprayojananiṣprayojanaśāstradarśanācchāstratvam eva prayojanavattāsaṃdehopadarśakam astu tathāpyalaṃ prayojanābhidhānena | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 11]
naivaṃ nahi sāmānyena prayojanasaṃdehaḥ prayojanaviśeṣārthinaṃ tathā pravartayati yathābhipretaprayojanaviśeṣaviṣayaḥ saṃdehaḥ abhipretaviśeṣaviṣayaśca saṃdeho na viśeṣaviṣayasmaraṇamantarā bhavati ato ye tāvad anavadhṛtāgniveśaprāmāṇyās teṣāṃ dhātusāmyasādhanamidaṃ śāstraṃ na vetyevam ākāraviśeṣasaṃdehotpādanārthaṃ prayojanaviśeṣābhidhānaṃ ye punaḥ paramarṣer agniveśasyādyata evāvadhṛtaprāmāṇyāsteṣāṃ tadabhihitaprayojanavattāvadhāraṇenaiva pravṛttir iti yuktaṃ prayojanābhidhānam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 12]
prayojanābhidhāyivākye tu svalpaprayatnabodhye prayojanasāmānyasaṃdehādeva pravṛttirupapannā na punaranekasaṃvatsarakleśabodhye śāstre | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 13]
tadevaṃ yaducyate prayojanābhidhāyivākyapravṛttāv api prayojanamabhidhātavyaṃ tathā cānavasthā iti tannirastaṃ bhavati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 14]
athetyādi sūtre 'thaśabdo brahmādipraṇītatantreṣv alpāyurmedhasāmarthānavadhāraṇasya tathābhīṣṭadevatānamaskāraśāstrakaraṇārthagurvājñālābhayor ānantarye prayukto'pi śāstrādau svarūpeṇa maṅgalaṃ bhavatyudakāharaṇapravṛttodakumbhadarśanam iva prasthitānām | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 15]
granthādau maṅgalasevānirastāntarāyāṇāṃ granthakartṛśrotṝṇām avighneneṣṭalābho bhavatīti yuktaṃ maṅgalopādānam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 16]
athaśabdasya maṅgalatve smṛtir oṃkāraś cāthaśabdaśca dvāv etau brahmaṇaḥ purā | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 17]
kaṇṭhaṃ bhittvā viniryātau tena māṅgalikāv ubhau iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 18]
śāstrāntare cādau maṅgalatvena dṛṣṭo'yamathaśabdaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 19]
yathā atha śabdānuśāsanam athāto dharmaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ vai ityādau | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 20]
abhīṣṭadevatānamaskārastu granthādau śiṣṭācāraprāptaḥ paramaśiṣṭenāgniveśena kṛta eva anyathā śiṣṭācāralaṅghanena śiṣṭatvameva na syād vyākhyānāntarāyabhayaśca tathā granthāviniveśitasyāpi namaskārasya pratyavāyāpahatvācca na granthaniveśanam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 21]
yathā ca gurvājñālābhānantaram etat tantrakaraṇaṃ tathā atha maitrīparaḥ puṇyam ityādau sphuṭameva | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 22]
granthakaraṇe ca gurvanumatipratipādanena granthasyopādeyatā pradarśitā bhavati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 23]
yat punaḥ śiṣyapraśnānantaryārthatvam athaśabdasya varṇyate tanna māṃ dhinoti nahi śiṣyān puro vyavasthāpya śāstraṃ kriyate śrotṛbuddhisthīkāre tu śāstrakaraṇaṃ yuktaṃ na ca buddhisthīkṛtāḥ praṣṭāro bhavanti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 24]
ataḥśabdo 'dhikāraprāgavadhyupadarśakaḥ ata ūrdhvaṃ yad upadekṣyāmo dīrghaṃjīvitīyaṃ taditi yadi vā hetau yena brahmādipraṇītāyurvedatantrāṇām uktena nyāyenotsambandhatvam iva ato hetor dīrghaṃjīvitīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti yojanīyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 25]
dīrghaṃjīvitīyam ityatra dīrghaṃjīvitaśabdo 'sminn astīti matvarthe adhyāyānuvākayor luk ca iti chapratyayaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 26]
yadi vā dīrghaṃjīvitaśabdam adhikṛtya kṛto grantho 'dhyāyarūpastantrarūpo vā ityasyāṃ vivakṣāyām adhikṛtya kṛte granthe ityadhikārāt śiśukrandayamasabha ityādinā chaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 27]
evamanyatrāpyevaṃjātīye mantavyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 28]
atra ca satyapi śabdāntare dīrghaṃjīvitaśabdenaiva saṃjñā kṛtā dīrghaṃjīvitaśabdasyaiva pravacanādau niveśāt praśastatvācca | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 29]
dīrghaṃjīvitaśabdo 'sminn asti iti dīrghaṃjīvitaśabdam adhikṛtya kṛto vā ityanayā vyutpattyā dīrghaṃjīvitīyaśabdas tantre 'dhyāye ca pravartanīyaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 30]
tena dīrghaṃjīvitīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma ityanena tantraṃ prati vyākhyānapratijñā labdhā bhavati punar dīrghaṃjīvitīyam iti padam āvartyādhyāyapadasamabhivyāhṛtam adhyāyavyākhyānapratijñāṃ lambhayati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 31]
dṛṣṭaṃ cāvṛtya padasya yojanaṃ yathā apāmārgataṇḍulīye gaurave śirasaḥ śūle pīnase ityādau śirasa iti padaṃ gaurave ityanena yujyate āvṛtya śūle ityanena ca | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 32]
ataśca yaducyate akṛtatantrapratijñasyādhyāyapratijñā ūnakāyamāneti tannirastaṃ bhavati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 33]
yadi vā adhyāyapratijñaivāstu tayaiva tantrapratijñāpyarthalabdhaiva na hy adhyāyas tantravyatiriktaḥ tenāvayavavyākhyāne tantrasyāpyavayavino vyākhyā bhavatyeva yathā aṅgulīgrahaṇena devadatto'pi gṛhīto bhavati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 34]
avayavāntaravyākhyānapratijñā tu na labhyate tāṃ tu pratyadhyāyameva kariṣyati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 35]
adhyāyamiti adhipūrvādiṅaḥ iṅaśca iti karmaṇi ghañā sādhyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 36]
tena adhīyate ityadhyāyaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 37]
na cānayā vyutpattyā prakaraṇacatuṣkasthānādiṣvatiprasaṅgaḥ yato yogarūḍheyam adhyāyasaṃjñādhyāyasya prakaraṇasamūhaviśeṣa eva dīrghaṃjīvitīyādilakṣaṇe paṅkajaśabdavadvartate na yogamātreṇa vartate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 38]
vakṣyati hi adhikṛtyeyamadhyāyanāmasaṃjñā pratiṣṭhitā iti nāmasaṃjñā yogarūḍhasaṃjñetyarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 39]
yadi vā karaṇādhikaraṇayor arthayoḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 40]
adhyāyanyāyodyāvasaṃhārāś ca itisūtreṇa nipātanād adhyāyapadasiddhiḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 41]
adhīyate'sminnanena vārthaviśeṣa ityadhyāyaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 42]
atiprasaktiniṣedhas tūktanyāyaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 43]
vyākhyāsyāma iti vyāṅpūrvāt khyāteﾱrṭā sādhyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 44]
cakṣiṅo hi prayoge 'nicchato 'pi vyākhyātuḥ kriyāphalasambandhasya durnivāratvena svaritañita ityādinātmanepadaṃ syāditi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 45]
vi iti viśeṣe viśeṣāśca vyāsasamāsādayaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 46]
āṅ ayaṃ kriyāyoge ye tu maryādāyām abhividhau vā āṅprayogaṃ manyante teṣām abhiprāyaṃ na vidmaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 47]
yato maryādāyāmabhividhau cāṅaḥ prātipadikena yogaḥ syāt yathā āsamudrakṣitīśānām ā pāṭalīputrād vṛṣṭo deva ityādau ihāpi ca tathā | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 48]
kriyāyogavirahe upasargāḥ kriyāyoge iti niyamād āṅa upasargatvaṃ na syāt tataścānupasargeṇāṅā vyavadhānād ver upasargasya prayogo na syāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 49]
yenāvyavahitaḥ sajātīyavyavahito vā dhātor upasargo bhavati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 50]
vyāṅor ubhayor apyanupasargatve tatsambandhocitabhūriprātipadikakalpanāgauravaprasaṅgaḥ syāt tasmāt kriyāyogitvam evāṅo nyāyyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 51]
atha ataḥ dīrghaṃ jīvitīyam adhyāyaṃ vi ā khyāsyāma ityaṣṭapadatvam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 1 52]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 2}
nanu kathamagniveśaḥ sakalapadārthāśeṣaviśeṣajñānavyākhyeyam āyurvedaṃ vyākhyāsyati yato na tāvad bheṣajādīnām aśeṣaviśeṣapratyakṣajñeyaḥ sarvapadārthānāṃ viśeṣāṇāṃ pratyakṣāviṣayatvāt anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ tu sarvapadārthāvadhāraṇaṃ duṣkarameva yata ekam eva madhu svarūpeṇa jīvayati mārayati coṣṇaṃ samaghṛtaṃ ca kaphaprakṛterhitamahitaṃ vātaprakṛteḥ anūpe sātmyamasātmyaṃ marau śīte sevyamasevyaṃ grīṣme hitam avṛddhe vṛddhe cāhitam alpaṃ guṇakaram ābādhakaram atyupayuktam āmatāṃ gatam udare upakramavirodhitvād ativibhramakaraṃ kākamācīyuktaṃ pakvanikucena ca sahopayuktaṃ maraṇāya athavā balavarṇavīryatejaupaghātāya bhavati ityevamādi tattad yuktaṃ tattacchataśaḥ karoti ata evaikasyaiva madhuno rūpaṃ yadānena prakāreṇa duradhigamaṃ tadātra kaiva kathā nikhilapadārthāśeṣaviśeṣajñānasya ajānaṃś ca vyācakṣāṇaḥ kathamupādeyavacana iti kṛtvā guror āptāt pratipannaṃ pratipādayiṣyāma iti darśayan tāmimāṃ śaṅkāṃ nirācikīrṣur gurūktānuvādarūpatāṃ svagranthasya darśayannāha iti ha smāha bhagavānātreya iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 2 1]
atra itiśabdo vakṣyamāṇārthaparāmarśakaḥ haśabdo'vadhāraṇe yathā na ha vai saśarīrasya priyāpriyayorapahatirastīti atra na heti naivetyarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 2 2.1]
atra smāha iti smaśabdaprayogena bhūtamātra eva liḍarthe laṭ sme iti laṭ na bhūtānadyatanaparokṣe ātreyopadeśasyāgniveśaṃ pratyaparokṣatvāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 2 3]
yathā ca bhūtamātre liḍ bhavati tathāca darśayiṣyāmaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 2 4]
bhagaṃ pūjitaṃ jñānaṃ tadvān yathoktam utpattiṃ pralayaṃ caiva bhūtānām āgatiṃ gatim | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 2 5]
vetti vidyāmavidyāṃ ca sa vācyo bhagavāniti yadi vā bhagaśabdaḥ samastaiśvaryamāhātmyādivacanaḥ yathoktam aiśvaryasya samagrasya vīryasya yaśasaḥ śriyaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 2 6]
jñānavairāgyayoścaiva ṣaṇṇāṃ bhaga itīṅganāḥ iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 2 7]
atrerapatyamātreyaḥ anena viśuddhavaṃśatvaṃ darśitaṃ bhavati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 2 8]
atrānye varṇayanti caturvidhaṃ sūtraṃ bhavati gurusūtraṃ śiṣyasūtraṃ pratisaṃskartṛsūtram ekīyasūtraṃ ceti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 2 9]
tatra gurusūtraṃ yathā naitad buddhimatā draṣṭavyam agniveśa ityādi pratisaṃskartṛsūtraṃ yathā tamuvāca bhagavānātreyaḥ ityādi śiṣyasūtraṃ yathā naitāni bhagavan pañcakaṣāyaśatāni pūryante ityādi ekīyasūtraṃ yathā kumārasya śiraḥ pūrvamabhinirvartata iti kumāraśirā bharadvājaḥ ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 2 10]
tenādyaṃ vyākhyānapratijñāsūtraṃ guroreva śiṣyasyāgniveśasya vyākhyāne 'nadhikāratvāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 2 11]
dvitīyaṃ ca sūtraṃ pratisaṃskartuḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 2 12.1]
itiśabdena ca prakāravācinā dīrghaṃjīvitīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāma iti parāmṛśyate tenāha smeti bhūtānadyatanaparokṣa eva bhavati pratisaṃskartāraṃ pratyātreyopadeśasya parokṣatvāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 2 12.2]
anena ca nyāyena tamuvāca bhagavānātreya ityādāv api liḍvidhir upapanno bhavati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 2 13]
suśrute ca yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ iti pratisaṃskartṛsūtramiti kṛtvā ṭīkākṛtā liḍvidhir upapāditaḥ iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 2 14]
atra brūmaḥ yattāvaduktaṃ śiṣyasyāgniveśasya vyākhyānānadhikārādidaṃ guroḥ sūtraṃ tanna nahi jātyā gurutvam asti yataḥ sa evātreyaḥ svagurum apekṣya śiṣyaḥ agniveśādīn apekṣya guruḥ evamagniveśo 'pi granthakaraṇakāle svabuddhisthīkṛtāñśiṣyān prati gururiti na kaścid doṣaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 2 15]
yatpunardvitīyasya pratisaṃskartṛsūtratayā bhūtānadyatanaparokṣe liḍvidhir upapādyate tatra vicāryaṃ kim idaṃ dvitīyaṃ sūtraṃ pūrvavākyaikatāpannaṃ na vā yadyekavākyatāpannaṃ tadā suśrute tathā vyākhyāsyāmo yathovāca dhanvantarir iti yojanīyaṃ tathāca tathā vyākhyāsyāma iti kriyaikavākyatāpannam uvācetipadaṃ na bhinnakartṛkaṃ bhavitum arhati tathā ca kuto liḍvidhiḥ atha naikatāpannaṃ tadā gaur aśvaḥ puruṣo hastītivannārthasaṃgatiḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 2 16]
kiṃca jatūkarṇādau pratisaṃskartṛśrutigandho 'pi nāsti tat kathaṃ nānāśrutaparipūrṇakaṇṭhaḥ śiṣyo jatūkarṇaḥ prāñjalir adhigamyovāca ityādau liḍvidhiḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 2 17]
anena nyāyena carake 'pi pratisaṃskartṛsūtrapakṣe liḍvidhirnāsti tasmāccarake 'gniveśaḥ suśrute suśruta eva sūtrāṇāṃ praṇetā kvacit kiṃcidarthaṃ stotuṃ nindituṃ vākhyāyikārūpaṃ purākalpaṃ darśayan kimapi sūtraṃ gurūktānuvādarūpatayā kimapyekīyamatānuvādarūpatayā likhati pratisaṃskartā tv ayaṃ granthaṃ pūrayati tadādyagranthakartṛtayaiva | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 2 18]
liḍvidhistu bhūtānadyatanamātra eva chandovihito bhāṣāyāmapi varṇanīyaḥ anyathā uvāceti padaṃ jatūkarṇādau na syāt tathā ca harivaṃśe dhanyopākhyāne māmuvāca iti tathā ahamuvāca iti ca na syāt yathā sa māmuvācāmbucaraḥ kūrmo mānuṣavat svayam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 2 19]
kimāścaryaṃ mayi mune dhanyaścāhaṃ kathaṃ vibho iti tathā svayaṃbhuvacanāt so 'haṃ vedān vai samupasthitaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 2 20]
uvāca caināṃścaturaḥ iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 2 21]
yadapi iti ha smāha ityatra itiśabdena pūrvasūtraṃ parāmṛśyate tanna yena dīrghaṃjīvitīyādisūtramātrasya tadarthasya vā gurūktatvapratipādane sati naivottaratrābhidheyābhidhānena nikhilatantrasya gurūktānuvādarūpatayā karaṇaṃ śrotṛśraddhākaraṇaṃ pratipāditaṃ bhavati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 2 22]
bhavati tu bhāvayituṃ yathā purā vyākhyātaṃ tasmāttadeva nyāyyamiti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 2 23]
agniveśasya vyākhyāsyāma iti bahuvacanam ekasminn apy asmadaḥ prayogādbahuvacanaprayogasya sādhutvāt sādhu hi vadanti vaktāro vayaṃ kariṣyāmaḥ iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 2 24]
bhagavānātreya ityatra tv ekavacananirdeśaḥ kṛtaḥ bhagavānityanenaivātreyasya gurorgauravasya darśitatvāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 2 25]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 15.1}
ke te maharṣaya ityāhāṅgirā ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 15.1 1]
bahvṛṣīṇām atra kīrtanaṃ granthādau pāpakṣayahetutvena tathāyurvedasyaivaṃvidhamahāpuruṣasevitatvena sevyatvopadarśanārthaṃ ceti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 15.1 2]
eṣu ca madhye kecid yāyāvarāḥ kecicchālīnāḥ kecidayonijāḥ evaṃprakārāśca sarve mīlitā boddhavyāḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 15.1 3]
bhikṣurityātreyaviśeṣaṇaṃ vakṣyati hi tanneti bhikṣur ātreyaḥ iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 15.1 4]
vaikhānasā iti karmaviśeṣaprayuktā saṃjñā | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 15.1 5]

{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 18.1}
dhāraṇāddharmaḥ sa cātmasamavetaḥ kāryadarśanānumeyaḥ arthaḥ suvarṇādiḥ kāmyata ita kāmo vanitāpariṣvaṅgādiḥ mokṣaḥ saṃsāravimokṣaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 18.1 1]
ārogyaṃ rogābhāvād dhātusāmyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 18.1 2]
mūlaṃ kāraṇam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 18.1 3]
uttamamiti pradhānaṃ tenārogyaṃ caturvarge pradhānaṃ kāraṇaṃ rogagṛhītasya kvacidapi puruṣārthe 'samarthatvād ityuktam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 18.1 4]
tasyāpahartāra iti ārogyasyāpahartāraḥ idam eva ca rogāṇām ārogyāpaharaṇaṃ yad anarthalābhaḥ na punar utpanno rogaḥ paścād ārogyam apaharati bhāvābhāvayoḥ parasparābhāvātmakatvāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 18.1 5]
śreyaso jīvitasya ceti śreyovajjīvitaṃ hitatvena sukhatvena cārthe daśamahāmūlīye vakṣyamāṇaṃ tasya jīvitasyāpahartāra iti yojanīyam aśreyojīvitamahitatvena duḥkhahetutayā cānupādeyam iti kṛtvā tadapaharaṇamiha noktam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 18.1 6]
atra sukhitajīvitopaghāto dharmādyupaghātenaiva labdhaḥ tena vayaṃ paśyāmaḥ śreyaḥśabdena sāmānye nābhyudayavācinā dharmādayo 'bhidhīyante jīvitaśabdena ca jīvitamātraṃ yato jīvitaṃ svarūpeṇaiva sarvaprāṇināṃ nirupādhyupādeyaṃ vacanaṃ hi ācakame ca brahmaṇa iyamātmā āśīḥ āyuṣmān bhūyāsam iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 18.1 7]
yattvatyantaduḥkhagṛhītasya jīvitaṃ jihāsitaṃ tatra duḥkhasyātyantajihāsitasyānyathā hātum aśakyatvāt priyamapi jīvitaṃ tyaktum icchati na svarūpeṇa | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 18.1 8]
antarāya iti dharmādisādhane boddhavyaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 18.1 9]
ayamiti rogaprādurbhāvarūpaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 18.1 10]
teṣāmiti rogāṇām | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 18.1 11]
śaraṇamiti rakṣitāram | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 18.1 12]
śaktatvācchakra ucyate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 18.1 13]
dhyānaṃ samādhiviśeṣaḥ tadupalabdhisādhanatvāccakṣur iva dhyānacakṣuḥ tena sa vakṣyati śamopāyaṃ yathāvad amaraprabhuḥ iti dhyānacakṣuṣā dadṛśuriti yojanā | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 18.1 14]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 23.2}
athaiteṣu madhye bharadvājaḥ katham indram upāgamad ityāha ka ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 23.2 1]
śacīpatim ityanena śacīsambhogavyāsaktam apyaham upāsituṃ kṣama iti bharadvājo darśayati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 23.2 2]
arthe prayojane | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 23.2 3]
niyujyeyaṃ vyāpārayeyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 23.2 4]
atreti prakṛtaprayojana eva atretiśabdo yasmādarthe | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 23.2 5]
yathā subhikṣam ityāgataḥ yasmāt subhikṣaṃ tasmādāgata ityarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 23.2 6]
niyojita iti caurādiko ṇica na hetau | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 23.2 7]
anena prakaraṇena bharadvājasyāyurvedāgame viśeṣeṇārthitvānna preraṇamiti darśitaṃ bhavati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 23.2 8]
provāceti samyaguvāca na tu praśabdaḥ prapañcārthaḥ padairalpair ityuktatvāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 23.2 9]
kasmāt padair alpair uvācetyāha matiṃ buddhvā vipulām iti yasmād vipulamatiṃ bharadvājaṃ pratipannavān tasmāt padair alpair uvāceti bhāvaḥ matiś ca bahuviṣayatvenopacārād vipulety ucyate sā ca matiḥ śuśrūṣāśravaṇagrahaṇadhāraṇohāpohatattvābhiniveśavatīha vipulā boddhavyā | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 23.2 10]
atra cendreṇa divyadṛśā bharadvājābhiprāyam agrata eva buddhvāyurveda upadiṣṭaḥ tena bharadvājasyendrapṛcchādīha na darśitaṃ kiṃvā bhūtam apīndrapṛcchādi granthavistarabhayād iha na likhitam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 23.2 11]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 24.2}
yādṛśo 'sāv alpapadair upadiṣṭa āyurvedastamāha hetvityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 24.2 1]
hetuliṅgauṣadhajñānamiti hetvādīni jñāyante 'neneti hetuliṅgauṣadhajñānaṃ yāvac cāyurvedavācyaṃ tāvaddhetvādyantarbhūtam ityarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 24.2 2]
hetugrahaṇena saṃnikṛṣṭaviprakṛṣṭavyādhihetugrahaṇaṃ liṅgagrahaṇena ca vyādher ārogyasya ca kṛtsnaṃ liṅgamucyate tena vyādhyārogye 'pi liṅgaśabdavācye yatastābhyāmapi hi talliṅgaṃ liṅgyata eva vakṣyati hi viṣamārambhamūlānāṃ jvara eko hi lakṣaṇam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 24.2 3]
viṣamārambhamūlādyair jvara eko nigadyate ityādi auṣadhagrahaṇena ca sarvapathyāvarodhaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 24.2 4]
śarīraṃ cātra hetau liṅge cāntarbhavati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 24.2 5]
svasthāturayoḥ paramutkṛṣṭamayanaṃ mārga iti svasthāturaparāyaṇam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 24.2 6]
kimanyo'yaṃ hetuliṅgauṣadhajñānarūpa āyurvedo brahmabuddhādāyurvedād utānanya ityāha trisūtram ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 24.2 7]
pitāmaho'pi yaṃ trisūtraṃ bubudhe tamindraḥ provāca | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 24.2 8]
trīṇi hetvādīni sūtryante yasmin yena vā tantrisūtram | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 24.2 9]
tatra sūcanāt sūtraṇāccārthasaṃtateḥ sūtram | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 24.2 10]
etena taṃ yathā brahmā trisūtraṃ bubudhe tathaiva hetuliṅgauṣadhajñānam indraḥ provācetyaviplutamāgamaṃ darśayati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 24.2 11]
bubudha iti na kṛtavān | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 24.2 12]
ata evoktaṃ śāśvataṃ nityam ityarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 24.2 13]
tacca nityatvaṃ sūtrasthānānte vyutpādanīyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 24.2 14]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 26.2}
athoddiṣṭam āyurvedaṃ kathaṃ gṛhītavān bharadvāja ityāha so 'nantetyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 26.2 1]
avidyamānāv antapārau yasyāsāv anantapāraḥ atra pāraśabdena gobalīvardanyāyenādir ucyate pāraśabdo hy ubhayor api nadīkūlayor vivakṣāvaśād vartate kiṃvā ananto mokṣaḥ pāram utkṛṣṭaṃ phalaṃ yasyāyurvedasyāsāv anantapāraḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 26.2 2]
vakṣyati hi cikitsā tu naiṣṭhikī yā vinopadhām iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 26.2 3]
atra naiṣṭhikī mokṣasādhanahetuḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 26.2 4]
trayo hetvādayaḥ skandharūpā yasya sa triskandhaḥ skandhaśca sthūlāvayavaḥ pravibhāgo vā | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 26.2 5]
tatraivāyurvedagrahaṇe mano yasya sa tanmanāḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 26.2 6]
mananājjñānaprakarṣaśālitvān muniḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 26.2 7]
etena yasmādayaṃ mahāmatis tanmanāḥ muniśca tenānantapāramapyāyurvedaṃ hetvādiskandhatrayamālambanaṃ kṛtvā yathāvadacirādeva pratipannavān ityāśayaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 26.2 8]
acirāditi acireṇa | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 26.2 9]
atra ca yathā brahmā trisūtraṃ bubudhe yathā cendro hetuliṅgauṣadhajñānaṃ provāca tathaiva bharadvājo'pi triskandhaṃ taṃ bubudhe ityanenāyurvedasyāviplutāgamatvam upadarśyate tena trisūtratriskandhayor na punaruktiḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 26.2 10]
teneti indrād gṛhītenāyurvedena | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 26.2 11]
amitamiti amitamivāmitam atidīrghatvāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 26.2 12]
āyuḥśabdaścāyuḥkāraṇe rasāyanajñāne boddhavyaḥ yenottarakālaṃ hi rasāyanopayogād ayaṃ bharadvājo'mitamāyuravāpsyati na ṛṣibhya āyurvedakathanāt pūrvaṃ rasāyanamācarati sma kiṃvā sarvaprāṇyupakārārthādhītāyurvedajanitadharmavaśāt tatkālam evāmitamāyur lebhe bharadvāja iti boddhavyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 26.2 13]
tacceti śrutaṃ yadā tamiti pāṭhaḥ tadā tam āyurvedam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 26.2 14]
anavaśeṣayanniti kārtsnyenetyarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 26.2 15]
āyurvedam adhītyānantaram evāyaṃ tamṛṣibhyo dattavān | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 26.2 16]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 29.2}

{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 31.2}
athetyādinā bharadvājaśiṣyasyātreyasya punarvasvaparanāmno 'gniveśādigurutāṃ darśayati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 31.2 1]
atra kecidbharadvājātreyayoraikyaṃ manyante tanna bharadvājasaṃjñayā ātreyasya kvacid api tantrapradeśe 'kīrtanāt hārīte cātreyādigurutayā bharadvāja uktaḥ śakrād aham adhītavān ityādinā mattaḥ punarasaṃkhyeyās trisūtraṃ triprayojanam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 31.2 2]
atrātreyādiparyantā viduḥ sapta maharṣayaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 31.2 3]
ātreyāddhārīta ṛṣir ityantena | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 31.2 4]

so 'śvinau tau sahasrākṣaṃ so 'triputrādikān munīn vā ityanenātreyasyendraśiṣyatvaṃ tadāyurvedasamutthānīyarasāyanapāde ādiśabdena vakṣyamāṇendraśiṣyatāyogāt samarthanīyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 31.2 6]

{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 43.2}
tasyetyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 43.2 1]
vedayatīti vedaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 43.2 2]
vedavidāṃ mata iti vedavidbhiḥ pūjitaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 43.2 3]
atha kasmād āyurvedalakṣaṇo vedaḥ puṇyatamo vedavidāṃ ca pūjita ityāha vakṣyata ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 43.2 4]
yaditi yasmāt evamuktaṃ bhavati yadanye ṛgvedādayaḥ prāyaḥ paralokahitamevārthaṃ vadanti tena puṇyāḥ puṇyatamaścāyamāyurvedo yad yasmānmanuṣyāṇāmubhayorapi lokayor yaddhitam āyurārogyasādhanaṃ dharmasādhanaṃ ca tadvakṣyate tenātiśayena puṇyatamastathā vedavidāṃ ca pūjita iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 43.2 5]
kecit vakṣyate yaḥ iti paṭhanti tatrāpi hetugarbhamiti vyākhyeyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 43.2 6]
jīvitapradātṛtvādāyurvedasya puṇyatamatvaṃ boddhavyaṃ yataś caturvargasādhanībhūtajīvitapradam eva sarvottamaṃ bhavati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 43.2 7]
ucyate ca na hi jīvitadānāddhi dānamanyadviśiṣyate iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 43.2 8]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 44.2}
sampratyāyurvedābhidheyatayā sūtrite sāmānyādau sāmānyasya prathamasūtritatvāt tathā sāmānyajñānamūlatvāccāyurvedapratipādyasya hetvādeḥ sāmānyamevāgre nirdiśati sarvadetyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 44.2 1]
sarvadā sarvasmin kāle nityage cāvasthike ca | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 44.2 2]
sarvabhāvānāmityatra sarvaśabdaḥ kṛtsnavācī bhavanti sattāmanubhavantīti bhāvā dravyaguṇakarmāṇītyarthaḥ natu bhavantyutpadyanta iti bhāvāḥ tathā sati pṛthivyādiparamāṇūnāṃ nityānāṃ sāmānyasya pārthivadvyaṇukādivṛddhaṃ kāryam asaṃgṛhītaṃ syāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 44.2 3]
sāmānyaṃ ca sāmānyamekatvakaram ityādinā vakṣyamāṇalakṣaṇam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 44.2 4]
vṛddhiḥ ādhikyaṃ tatkāraṇaṃ vṛddhikāraṇam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 44.2 5]
etacca sāmānyaṃ sāmānyavato māṃsadravyāder vṛddhikāraṇasya lakṣaṇatvena vṛddhikāraṇamityuktam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 44.2 6]
yato na sāmānyaṃ māṃsatvādijātirūpaṃ vṛddhau kāraṇaṃ bhavati tathāhi sati sāmānyaṃ bhāsatvarūpaṃ yathā vardhake bhojyarūpe māṃse'sti tathā śarīradhāturūpe vardhanīye'pyasti tataśca nityaṃ māṃsatvasambandhād amāṃsādānām api māṃsena vardhitavyaṃ tasmādvṛddhikāraṇalakṣaṇatvena sāmānyaṃ vṛddhikāraṇamityuktam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 44.2 7]
ata eva vaiśeṣike'pyuktaṃ trayāṇām akāryatvam akāraṇatvaṃ ca iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 44.2 8]
atra trayāṇāmiti sāmānyaviśeṣasamavāyānām | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 44.2 9]
ye tu samānam eva sāmānyam iti kṛtvā dravyādyeva sāmānyaśabdenābhidadhati teṣāṃ mate sāmānyaṃ ca viśeṣaṃ ca ityādigranthoktasya sāmānyasya na kiṃcidanenoktaṃ syād ityasaṃbandhārthatvaṃ prakaraṇasya syāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 44.2 10]
etacca vṛddhikāraṇatvaṃ sāmānyasya na lakṣaṇaṃ kiṃ tarhyāyurvedopayoginā dharmeṇa nirdeśaḥ lakṣaṇaṃ tu sāmānyamekatvakaram iti kariṣyati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 44.2 11]
evaṃ dravyādāvapi coddeśānantaraṃ nirdeśaṃ kariṣyati khādīnyātmā ityādinā tato | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 1, 44.2 12]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 2}
mātrāśitīye mātrāvadāhārasya balādihetutvaṃ pratipāditaṃ tacca ṛtusātmyamapekṣya kṛtasyāhārasya bhavati tena ṛtupravibhāgapūrvakam ṛtusātmyābhidhāyakaṃ tasyāśitīyaṃ brūte | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 2 1]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 3.2}
aśitādyāditi aśitapītalīḍhajagdhāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 3.2 1]
balaṃ varṇaśceti cakāreṇa pūrvādhyāyoktasukhāyuṣī api gṛhyete yadi vā balavarṇābhyāmeva nāntarīyakaṃ kṛtsnaṃ dhātusāmyakāryaṃ sukhādi gṛhyate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 3.2 2]
viditamityanena samyagjñānapūrvakam ṛtusātmyānuṣṭhānaṃ darśayati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 3.2 3]
ceṣṭāgrahaṇena vyavāyavyāyāmābhyaṅgādīnāṃ grahaṇam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 3.2 4]
ceṣṭāhāravyapāśrayaṃ ceṣṭāhāragocaram | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 3.2 5]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 4.2}
ṛtujñānamantarā ṛtusātmyajñānaṃ na sambhavatītyṛtūnām upayuktasvarūpajñānārthamāha ihetyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 4.2 1]
ṛtupratipādanaprastāve saṃvatsaraṃ vidyāditi saṃvatsarapratipādanamṛtūnāmeva militānāṃ saṃvatsaratvapratipādanārtham | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 4.2 2]
melakaśca buddhyā vyavahriyate na tu paramārthataḥ ṛtūnāṃ melako'sti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 4.2 3]
ṛtūnāṃ saṃvatsarātmakatvaṃ punaḥ punasta evartavaḥ parāvartanta iti jñānārthamavaśyaṃ pratipādanīyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 4.2 4]
iheti iha prakaraṇe ṣaḍaṅgaṃ vidyāt anyatra tu rogabhiṣagjitīyādau tattatkāryavaśād anyathāpi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 4.2 5]
uktaṃ ca śītoṣṇavarṣalakṣaṇaḥ kāla ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 4.2 6]
ṣaḍaṅgamiti samāhāre dviguḥ ṛtuvyatirekeṇa saṃvatsarasyāvidyamānatvāt yadi vā samudāyibhyo'nyaḥ samudāya ityāśritya bahuvrīhiḥ kāryaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 4.2 7]
tatreti ṛtuvibhāgakathane | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 4.2 8]
udaguttarāṃ diśaṃ prati ayanaṃ gamanamudagayanam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 4.2 9]
ādadāti kṣapayati pṛthivyāḥ saumyāṃśaṃ prāṇināṃ ca balamityādānam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 4.2 10]
trīn śiśirādīnityanenaiva labdhe'pi grīṣmāntatve grīṣmāntāniti śiśirasyādiriti vigrahasya tathādiśabdasya prakāravācitāyāḥ pratiṣedhārtham | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 4.2 11]
evaṃ hemantāntāniti ca vyākhyeyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 4.2 12]
dakṣiṇāṃ diśaṃ prati ayanaṃ dakṣiṇāyanam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 4.2 13]
visṛjati janayati āpyamaṃśaṃ prāṇināṃ ca balamiti visargaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 4.2 14]
saṃjñāpraṇayanaṃ ca vyavahārārthaṃ niruktipratīyamānārthapratipādanārthaṃ ca | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 4.2 15]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 5.2}
visargadharmaṃ nirdiśati visarge punarityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 5.2 1]
yadyapi cādānamādau paṭhitaṃ tathāpi pratilomatantrayuktyādau visargaguṇakathanaṃ yadi vā prathamamādānasyottarāyaṇarūpasya praśastatvādagre'bhidhānam iha tu visargasya balajanakatvenābhipretatvādagre 'bhidhānam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 5.2 2]
nātirūkṣā iti saumyavisargakālasambandhena mandīkṛtaraukṣyāḥ pravāntīti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 5.2 3]
itare punarādāna iti apraśāntātirūkṣāśca āgneyādānasambandhāhitarūkṣatvāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 5.2 4]
somaścetyādi prakṛtena visargeṇa sambadhyate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 5.2 5]
avyāhatabala iti kālamārgameghavātādibhistadā sūryasya somaparipanthino hatabalatvāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 5.2 6]
śiśirābhiḥ śītābhiḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 5.2 7]
śaśvaditi chedaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 5.2 8]
saumyaḥ somaguṇapradhānaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 5.2 9]
āgneyam agniguṇapradhānam apratihatabalatvenetyarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 5.2 10]
nanvetāvataivādityacandravātānāṃ balavattvamabalavattvaṃ ca kathaṃ bhavatītyāha tāvetāvityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 5.2 11]
kālo devatārūpaḥ sa ca nityarūpo'pi prāṇināmadṛṣṭena nānārūpeṇa gṛhītaḥ san kadācit sūryabalavāyubalasomabalādīn karoti svabhāvaḥ sūryasya saumyāṃśakṣayakartṛtvādir vāyor virūkṣaṇādiḥ somasyāpyāyanādiḥ mārgo dakṣiṇa uttaraśca tatra dakṣiṇaḥ karkaṭādayo dhanurantāḥ makarādiruttaraḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 5.2 12]
ete ca kālasvabhāvamārgaparigrahā yathāsambhavaṃ boddhavyāḥ na hi some mārgaparigrahaḥ kiṃcid viśeṣamāvahati vāyośca mārgaparigraha eva nāsti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 5.2 13]
parigṛhītāḥ sambaddhāḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 5.2 14]
kālartvādīnāṃ nirvṛtipratyayabhūtā niṣpattikāraṇabhūtāḥ upadiśyante ācāryaiḥ iti śeṣaḥ kālaḥ saṃvatsaro'yanadvayaṃ ca ṛtavaḥ śiśirādayaḥ dehasya balaṃ dehabalam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 5.2 15]
anye tu bruvate saṃvatsarasyāyanadvayasya ca ṛtumelakarūpatvād ṛtugrahaṇe naiva grahaṇaṃ labdhaṃ tena kālagrahaṇaviśeṣaṇaṃ tena kālarūpaḥ ṛturiti strīṇāmevārtavadarśanaṃ yadṛtustadvyāvartyate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 5.2 16]
pratyayabhūtā ityatra bhūtaśabda upamāne | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 5.2 17]
kecid vyākhyānayanti arkavāyū ityekatayā paṭhitvā somaśca iti yat pṛthak paṭhati tenārkvāyvor militayor ādānaṃ prati kāraṇatvaṃ visargaṃ prati pṛthageva somasya kāraṇatvamiti darśayati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 5.2 18]
evaṃ balaharaṇabalakaraṇādiṣvapi boddhavyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 5.2 19]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 6}
tatretyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 6 1]
ādadāna ucchoṣayan | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 6 2]
jagataḥ sthāvarajaṅgamasya | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 6 3]
snehaṃ sāraṃ saumyabhāgamityarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 6 4]
na kevalaṃ raviḥ vāyavaśca śoṣayantaḥ snehamiti sambandhaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 6 5]
tīvrāśca rūkṣāśca tīvrarūkṣāḥ yadi vā tīvraṃ raukṣyaṃ yeṣāṃ te tīvrarūkṣāḥ etaccādāne tīvreṇa raviṇā sambandhād vāyorbhavati yogavāhitvādvāyoḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 6 6]
uktaṃ hi yogavāhī paraṃ vāyuḥ saṃyogādubhayārthakṛd ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 6 7]
yathākramamiti śiśire raukṣyamalpaṃ tiktaṃ rasamalpaṃ ca daurbalyaṃ tathā vasante madhyaṃ raukṣyaṃ kaṣāyaṃ rasaṃ madhyaṃ daurbalyaṃ tathā grīṣme prakṛṣṭaṃ raukṣyaṃ kaṭukaṃ rasaṃ mahacca daurbalyaṃ darśayati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 6 8]
yadyapi ca kaṣāyo raso rūkṣatamaḥ kaṭukaśca rūkṣataraḥ yaduktaṃ raukṣyāt kaṣāyo rūkṣāṇāṃ pravaro madhyamaḥ kaṭuḥ ityādi raukṣyaprakarṣaśca grīṣme madhyabalaṃ ca raukṣyaṃ vasante tathāpi vāyvagniguṇabāhulyāt kaṭukasya vāyvagniguṇabahule grīṣmakāla evotpattiḥ pavanapṛthivyutkarṣavati tu vasante pavanapṛthivyutkarṣajanyasya kaṣāyasyotpattiḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 6 9]
yaduktaṃ vāyvagniguṇabhūyiṣṭhatvāt kaṭukaḥ pavanapṛthivyatirekāt kaṣāyaḥ iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 6 10]
pṛthivyādyutkarṣaśca kālaviśeṣaprabhāvakṛtaḥ kāryadarśanādunneyaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 6 11]
abhivardhayanta iti vacanādyathāsvakāle tiktādīnāmabhivṛddhiḥ sūcyate tena na tadaikarasatvam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 6 12]
atra ca kramavad raukṣyotpattitiktādyutpattī api daurbalyotpattau kāraṇaṃ yato raukṣyamutpādayanta iti tiktakaṣāyakaṭukān abhivardhayanta iti ca hetugarbhaviśeṣaṇadvayaṃ kṛtvā daurbalyam āvahantītyuktam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 6 13]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 7}
varṣetyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 7 1]
tuśabdaḥ pūrvapakṣavyāvṛttau | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 7 2]
dakṣiṇābhimukhe dakṣiṇāśāṃ gantumudyata evārke tena viṣuvadudayopalakṣitamadhyadeśād uttareṇa vartamāno'pi raviryadaiva dakṣiṇāśāṃ gantumudyato bhavati tadaiva kṣīyamāṇabalo bhavati uttarāśāgamanaprakarṣāhitabalaprakarṣatayā tu stokastokakramāpacīyamānabalo'pi tathā durbalo na lakṣyate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 7 3]
evamuttarāyaṇe'pi vyākhyeyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 7 4]
kālaḥ pūrvaṃ vyākhyātaḥ mārga iha dakṣiṇābhimukhaḥ meghasya vāto meghavātaḥ varṣaṇaṃ varṣaḥ etairabhihatapratāpe'rka iti sambandhaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 7 5]
vātastviha meghasambandhāhitaśaityo'rkatāpaparipanthī bhavati śaśino'vyāhatabalatvaṃ sūryasya paripanthino'bhihatapratāpatvād anuguṇamedhavātavarṣaṇayogācca | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 7 6]
jagati sthāvarajaṅgame | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 7 7]
atra ca pṛthivyagnibhūyiṣṭhatvādamlaḥ salilāgnibhūyiṣṭhatvāllavaṇa ityuktaṃ tat kathaṃ saumye visarge tayoścāgneyayorutpāda iti na vācyam yato balaprakarṣavato 'rkasya kṣīyamāṇabalasyāpi viṣuvaparyantaṃ balavattvamastyeveti vyutpāditameva | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 7 8]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 8.3}
samprati śiśirādau balahrāsaḥ pratipādito varṣādau ca balotkarṣas tatra śiśire durbalā varṣāsu balavantaḥ prāṇino bhavantītyādidurgrahaṃ niṣeddhum āha ādāvante cetyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 8.3 1]
visargasyādau varṣāsu ādānasyānte grīṣme daurbalyaṃ prakarṣaṃ prāptaṃ nirdiśediti sambandhaḥ tathā madhye visargasya śaradi ādānasya madhye vasante madhyaṃ nātikṣīṇaṃ nātivṛddhaṃ balaṃ vinirdiśediti yojyaṃ tathānte visargasya hemante agre ca prathame ādānasya śiśire śreṣṭhaṃ balaṃ vinirdiśediti yojanā | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 8.3 2]
evaṃ manyate visargaprakarṣāhitabalaprakarṣaḥ puruṣa ādānasyādau śiśire stokakṣīyamāṇabalo'pi balavān bhavati yathā pauṣamāsāntāhitavṛddhiprakarṣā niśā māghaphālgunayoḥ kṣīyamāṇāpi divasānmahatyeva bhavati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 8.3 3]
anena nyāyena varṣāsu daurbalyaṃ vasantaśaradośca madhyamaṃ balaṃ boddhavyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 8.3 4]
evaṃ kālarturasadehabalakāraṇatvam arkādīnāṃ vyavasthāpitaṃ doṣakāraṇatvaṃ tvagre ṛtuvidhānanirdeśe'bhidhāsyate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 6, 8.3 5]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 11, 43}
āyatanānyupasaṃharati itītyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 11, 43 1]
vikārāṇāṃ hetavo bhavantīti sambandhaḥ tathā samayogayuktāḥ samyagyogayuktāḥ prakṛtihetavo bhavantīti yojyaṃ prakṛtiḥ ārogyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 11, 43 2]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 2}
pūrvādhyāye rogāḥ svarūpamārgabāhyakāraṇabheṣajair abhihitāḥ upayuktajñānās tatkāraṇavātādayo bahuvācyatvān noktāḥ ataḥ samprati pṛthakprakaraṇe te 'bhidhīyante vātakalākalīye tatrāpi prādhānyād vāyureva prathamamucyate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 2 1.1]
kalā guṇaḥ yaduktaṃ ṣoḍaśakalam iti akalā guṇaviruddho doṣaḥ tena vātakalākalīyo vātaguṇadoṣīya ityarthaḥ yadi vā kalā sūkṣmo bhāgas tasyāpi kalā kalākalā tasyāpi sūkṣmo bhāga ityarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 2 1.2]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 3}
atrānekarṣivacanarūpatayā vātādiguṇavacanaṃ bahvṛṣisammatidarśanārthaṃ tantradharmaitihyayuktatvakaraṇārthaṃ ca | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 3 1.1]
asaṃghātamiti pittaśleṣmavad avayavasaṃghātarahitam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 3 1.2]
anavasthitamiti calasvabhāvam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 3 1.3]
anāsādyeti calatvenānibiḍāvayatvena ceti mantavyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 3 1.4]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 4}
rūkṣādayo bhāvapradhānāḥ tena rūkṣatvādayo guṇā mantavyāḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 4 1.1]
dāruṇatvaṃ calatvaṃ calatvāt evaṃ dīrghaṃjīvitīyoktaṃ calatvamuktaṃ bhavati yadi vā dāruṇatvaṃ śoṣaṇatvātkāṭhinyaṃ karotīti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 4 1.2]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 5}
kumāraśirā iti bharadvājaviśeṣaṇam ātreyagurubharadvājaniṣedhārtham | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 5 1.1]
evamprabhāvairiti prabhāvād raukṣyādikārakair dhāvanajāgaraṇādibhiḥ prabhāvābhidhānaṃ ca karmaṇāṃ nirguṇatvāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 5 1.2]
abhyasyamānairiti asakṛtprayuktaiḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 5 1.3]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 7.2}
śarīrāṇāmiti śarīrāvayavānām | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 7.2 1.1]
śuṣirakarāṇi randhrakarāṇi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 7.2 1.2]
āśrayamiti samānaguṇasthānam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 7.2 1.3]
āpyāyamānaḥ cīyamānaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 7.2 1.4]
dāruṇaviparīto mṛduḥ śuṣiraviparīto ghanaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 7.2 1.5]
asajyamānaḥ anavatiṣṭhamānaḥ kṣīyamāṇāvayava iti yāvat | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 7.2 1.6]
etenaitaduktaṃ bhavati yadyapi vāyunā vātakāraṇānāṃ vātaśamanānāṃ vā tathā sambandho nāsti tathāpi śarīrasambaddhais tair vātasya śarīracāriṇaḥ sambandho bhavati tataśca vātasya samānaguṇayogādvṛddhir viparītaguṇayogācca hrāsa upapanna eveti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 7.2 1.7]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 8.5}
śarīrāśarīracarasyeti vātasvarūpakathanaṃ tena śarīreṣu carata iti bahiḥ śarīrebhyo veti ca punaruktaṃ na bhavati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 8.5 1]
atrāvayavāniti vadan kārtsnyābhidhānamaśakyaṃ bahuprapañcatvāditi darśayati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 8.5 2]
sādhayitvā pratipādya | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 8.5 3]
vātakarmasu pratyakṣāṇi vacanādīni manaḥpreraṇādyanumeyaṃ garbhākṛtikaraṇādyāgamagamyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 8.5 4]
tantraṃ śarīraṃ yad uktaṃ tantrayantreṣu bhinneṣu tamo'ntyaṃ pravivikṣatām iti tadeva yantraṃ yadi vā tantrasya yantraṃ saṃdhayaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 8.5 5]
prāṇādyātmā prāṇādisvarūpaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 8.5 6]
ceṣṭāviśeṣaṇam uccāvacānāṃ vividhānām ityarthaḥ kiṃvā śubhāśubhānāmityarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 8.5 7]
niyantā anīpsite viṣaye pravartamānasya manasaḥ praṇetā ca manasa evepsite 'rthe | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 8.5 8]
udyojakaḥ prerakaḥ kiṃvā udyogakāraka iti pāṭhaḥ so 'pyabhinnārthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 8.5 9]
abhivoḍhevābhivoḍhā sarvendriyārthagrāhakatvena taccāsya vāyumayena sparśanendriyeṇa sarvendriyāṇāṃ vyāpakatvāt pūrvādhyāyapratipāditena nyāyena boddhavyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 8.5 10]
vyūhakaraḥ saṃghātakaro racanākara iti yāvat | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 8.5 11]
prakṛtiḥ kāraṇaṃ śabdakāraṇatvaṃ ca vāyor nityam ākāśānupraveśāt uktaṃ hi khādīnyabhidhāya teṣāmekaguṇaḥ pūrvo guṇavṛddhiḥ pare pare iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 8.5 12]
tathā punaruktaṃ khādīnyabhidhāya viṣṭaṃ hy aparaṃ pareṇa iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 8.5 13]
śravaṇamūlatvaṃ vāyoḥ karṇaśaṣkulīracanāviśeṣe vyāpriyamāṇatvāt mūlaṃ pradhānakāraṇam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 8.5 14]
utsāhaḥ kāryeṣūdyogo manasaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 8.5 15]
yoniḥ abhivyaktikāraṇam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 8.5 16]

bhettā kartā etacca śarīrotpattikāle | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 8.5 18]
bhūtaśabdaḥ svarūpavacanaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 8.5 19]
upaghātāyeti chedaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 8.5 20]
garbhāniti vikṛtim āpādayatyatikālaṃ dhārayatītyanena ca sambadhyate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 8.5 21]
ādityādīnāṃ saṃtānenāvicchedena gatividhānaṃ saṃtānagatividhānam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 8.5 22]
srotasāmiti nadīnām | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 8.5 23]
pravibhāgo vibhaktalakṣaṇam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 8.5 24]
dhātūnāmiti pṛthivyādīnāṃ dhātavaḥ kāryadravyāṇi prastarādīni mānaṃ parimāṇaṃ saṃsthānamākṛtiḥ tayorvyaktirabhivyaktiḥ tatra kāraṇamiti yāvat | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 8.5 25]
bījasya śālyādeḥ abhisaṃskāro 'ṅkurajananaśaktiḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 8.5 26]
avikledaḥ pākakālād arvāg aviklinnatvam upaśoṣaṇaṃ ca pākena yavādīnāmārdrāṇāmeva avikledopaśoṣaṇe śasyānāmeva | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 8.5 27]

visarjanaṃ visargaḥ sa ca pṛthaṅnīhārādibhiḥ sambadhyate nīhāraḥ śiśirasamūhaḥ nirhrādo meghaṃ vinā garjitam aśaniḥ vajrabhedo'gniḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 8.5 33]
asaṃghātaḥ anutpādo 'nupacayo vā | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 8.5 34]
upasargaḥ marakādiprādurbhāvaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 8.5 35]
meghasūryetyādau visargaḥ sṛṣṭiḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 8.5 36]
vāyur iha devatārūpo'bhipretaḥ tena tasya bhūtalacaturyugāntakarānilakaraṇam aviruddham evaṃ yadanyad apy anupapadyamānaṃ vāyos tadapi devatārūpatvenaiva samādheyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 8.5 37.1]

{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 11}
pittāntargata iti vacanena śarīre jvālādiyuktavahniniṣedhena pittoṣmarūpasya vahneḥ sadbhāvaṃ darśayati na tu pittādabhedaṃ pitte nāgnimāndyasya grahaṇyadhyāye vakṣyamāṇatvāt tathā pittaharasya sarpiṣo'gnivardhanatvenoktatvāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 12, 11 1]

{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 20, 3}

prakṛtiriha svabhāvaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 20, 3 1.2]

evaṃ caturvidhatvādi pratipādya punaḥ prakārāntareṇāparisaṃkhyeyatāṃ rogāṇāmāha vikārā ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 20, 3 1.4]
punariti vakṣyamāṇaprakārāntareṇa | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 20, 3 1.5]
prakṛtiḥ pratyāsannaṃ kāraṇaṃ vātādi adhiṣṭhānaṃ dūṣyaṃ liṅgāni lakṣaṇāni āyatanāni bāhyahetavo duṣṭāhārācārāḥ eṣāṃ vikalparūpo viśeṣo vikalpaviśeṣaḥ teṣāmaparisaṃkhyeyatvāditi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 20, 3 1.6]
atra doṣāḥ saṃsargāṃśāṃśavikalpādibhirasaṃkhyeyāḥ dūṣyāstu śarīrāvayavā aṇuśaḥ parasparamelakena vibhajyamānā asaṃkhyeyāḥ liṅgāni kṛtsnavikāragatānyasaṃkhyeyānyeva āviṣkṛtāni tu tantre kathitāni hetavaścāvāntaraviśeṣādasaṃkhyeyāḥ pravyaktā eva | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 20, 3 1.7]
kecit punaḥ eṣāṃ vikārāḥ iti paṭhanti sa tu pāṭho nānumatastāvat yadi ca syāttadā dehamanaḥpratyavamarśakam eṣām iti padaṃ bahuvacanaṃ tu manaḥśarīrayorbahutvavivakṣayā | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 20, 3 1.8]

{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 20, 8}

{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 20, 11.2}

bādhiryaṃ śabdamātrasyaivāśravaṇam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 20, 11.2 15]

{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 7.2}

{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 8.9}
eka evetyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 8.9 1]

tatra dravyabhedād ādhārabhedenāśritasyāpi rasasya bhedo bhavati āśrayo hi kāraṇaṃ kāraṇabhedācca kāryabhedo 'vaśyaṃ bhavatītyarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 8.9 14]

bhedastathāpi nākhyātuṃ sarasvatyāpi śakyate iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 8.9 18]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3}
siddhāntaṃ punarvasuvacanenāha ṣaḍ evetyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 1]

tayormiśrībhāvāditi karmaṇor amūrtayor miśrībhāvānupapattau tadādhārayor dravyayor miśrībhāvāditi boddhavyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 5]

pañcamahābhūtetyādau tuśabdo 'vadhāraṇe tena āśrayā eva na rasā ityarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 9]
kiṃbhūtā bhaumādayo bhūtavikārā āśrayā ityāha prakṛtivikṛtivicāradeśakālavaśā iti vaśaśabdo 'dhīnārthaḥ sa ca prakṛtyādibhiḥ pratyekaṃ yojyaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 10]
tatra prakṛtivaśā yathā mudgāḥ kaṣāyā madhurāśca santaḥ prakṛtyā laghavaḥ etaddhi lāghavaṃ na rasavaśaṃ tathāhi sati kaṣāyamadhuratvād gurutvaṃ syāt vikṛtivaśaṃ ca vrīher lājānāṃ laghutvaṃ tathā saktusiddhapiṇḍakānāṃ ca gurutvaṃ vicāraṇā vicāro dravyāntarasaṃyoga ityarthaḥ tena vicāraṇāvaśaṃ yathā madhusarpiṣī saṃyukte viṣaṃ tathā viṣaṃ cāgadasaṃyuktaṃ svakāryavyatiriktakāryakāri deśo dvividho bhūmir āturaśca tatra bhūmau śvetakāpotī valmīkādhirūḍhā viṣaharī tathā himavati bheṣajāni mahāguṇāni bhavanti śarīradeśe yathā sakthimāṃsād gurutaraṃ skandhakroḍaśiraspadām ityādi kālavaśaṃ tu yathā mūlakamadhikṛtyoktaṃ tadbālaṃ doṣaharaṃ vṛddhaṃ tridoṣaṃ tathā yathartupuṣpaphalam ādadīta ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 11]
atra caikaprakaraṇoktā ye 'nuktās te cakārāt svabhāvādiṣvevāntarbhāvanīyāḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 12]
yaduktaṃ caraḥ śarīrāvayavāḥ svabhāvo dhātavaḥ kriyāḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 13]
liṅgaṃ pramāṇaṃ saṃskāro mātrā cāsmin parīkṣyate iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 14]
tatra caraśarīrāvayavadhātūnāṃ deśena grahaṇaṃ mātrā vicāre praviśati śeṣaṃ svabhāve tathā rasavimāne vakṣyamāṇaṃ cātrāpraviṣṭam āhāraviśeṣāyatanam antarbhāvanīyaṃ yathāsambhavam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 15]
snigdharūkṣādyā ityatrādigrahaṇenānuktā api tīkṣṇamṛdvādayo na rasāḥ kiṃtu dravyaguṇāḥ pṛthageveti darśayati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 16]
kṣaraṇāt adhogamanakriyāyogāt kṣāro dravyaṃ nāsau rasaḥ rasasya hi niṣkriyasya kriyānupapannetyarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 17]
kṣaraṇaṃ ca kṣārasya pānīyayuktasyādhogamanena vadanti hi laukikāḥ kṣāraṃ srāvayāmaḥ iti śāstraṃ ca chittvā chittvāśayāt kṣāraḥ kṣaratvāt kṣārayatyadhaḥ iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 18]
hetvantaram āha dravyaṃ tadanekarasotpannam iti anekarasebhyo muṣkakāpāmārgādibhya utpannam anekarasotpannaṃ yataś cānekarasotpannam ata evānekarasaṃ kāraṇaguṇānuvidhāyitvāt kāryaguṇasyeti bhāvaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 19]
anekarasatvamevāha kaṭukalavaṇabhūyiṣṭham iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 20]
bhūyiṣṭhaśabdenāpradhānarasāntarasambandho 'stīti darśayati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 21]
hetvantaram āha anekendriyārthasamanvitam iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 22]
kṣāro hi sparśena gandhena cānvitaḥ tena dravyaṃ rase hi guṇe na sparśo nāpi gandha iti bhāvaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 23]
hetvantaramāha karaṇābhinirvṛttamiti karaṇena bhasmaparisrāvaṇādinābhinirvṛttaṃ kṛtam ityarthaḥ na raso 'nena prakāreṇa kriyata iti bhāvaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 24]
avyaktarasapakṣaṃ niṣedhayati avyaktībhāva ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 25]
avyaktībhāva ityabhūtatadbhāve cvipratyayena rasānāṃ madhurādīnāṃ vyaktānām eva kvacidādhāre 'vyaktatvaṃ nānyo madhurādibhyo 'vyaktarasa ityarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 26]
rasānāmiti madhurādīnāṃ ṣaṇṇām | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 27]
prakṛtāv ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 28]
prakṛtau kāraṇe jala ityarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 29]
avyaktatvaṃ ca rasasāmānyamātropalabdhir madhurādiviśeṣaśūnyā sā ca jale bhavati yata uktaṃ jalaguṇakathane suśrute vyaktarasatā rasadoṣaḥ iti ihāpi ca avyaktarasaṃ ca iti vakṣyati loke'pi cāvyaktarasaṃ dravyamāsvādya vaktāro vadanti jalasyevāsya raso na kaścin madhurādir vyakta iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 30]
viśeṣamadhurādyanupalabdhiś cānudbhūtatvena | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 31]
yathā dūrād avijñāyamānaviśeṣavarṇe vastuni rūpasāmānyapratītir bhavati na śuklatvādiviśeṣabuddhiḥ tathānurase 'vyaktībhāvo bhavati pradhānaṃ vyaktaṃ rasamanugato 'vyaktatvenetyanurasaḥ yathā veṇuyave madhure kaṣāyo 'nurasaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 32]
yaduktaṃ rūkṣaḥ kaṣāyānuraso madhuraḥ kaphapittahā iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 33]
anurasasamanvita iti sarvānurasayukte yathā viṣe vacanaṃ hi uṣṇam anirdeśyarasam ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 34]
kiṃvā aṇurasasamanvite iti pāṭhas tena aṇurasenaikena maricena śarkarāpānake kaṭutvam avyaktaṃ syāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 35]
aparisaṃkhyeyapakṣaṃ dūṣayati aparītyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 36]
teṣāmiti rasānām aparisaṃkhyeyatvaṃ na yuktam āśrayādīnāṃ bhāvānāmiti āśrayaguṇakarmasaṃsvādānām viśeṣāparisaṃkhyeyatvāditi āśrayādibhedasyāparisaṃkhyeyatvāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 37]
atra hetumāha ekaiko'pi hītyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 38]
eṣāmāśrayaguṇakarmasaṃsvādānāṃ viśeṣān ekaiko 'pi madhurādir āśrayate na ca tasmād āśrayādibhedād anyatvam āśritasya madhurāder bhavati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 39]
evaṃ manyate yadyapi śālimudgaghṛtakṣīrādayo madhurasyāśrayā bhinnāḥ tathāpi tatra madhuratvajātyākrānta eka eva raso bhavati balākākṣīrakārpāsādiṣu śuklavarṇa iva | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 40]
tathā guṇānāṃ gurupicchilasnigdhādīnāmanyatve 'pi karmaṇāṃ vā rasādivardhanāyurjananavarṇakaratvādīnāṃ bhinnatve satyapi na madhurarasasyānyatvaṃ yata eka eva madhuras tattadguṇayukto bhavati tatkarmakārī ceti ko virodhaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 41]
tathā madhurasyāvāntarāsvādabhede 'pi madhuratvajātyanatikramaḥ kṛṣṇavarṇāvāntarabhede yathā kṛṣṇatvānatikramaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 42]
nanu maivaṃ bhavatv aparisaṃkhyeyatvaṃ rasānāṃ parasparasaṃyogāt tu ya āsvādaviśeṣaḥ sa kāryaviśeṣakaro 'pi na hi yanmadhurāmlena kriyate tanmadhureṇa vāmlena vā śakyam atastena parasparasaṃyogenāparisaṃkhyeyatvaṃ bhaviṣyatītyāha parasparetyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 43]
saṃsṛṣṭam iti bhāve ktaḥ tena parasparasaṃsargabhūyiṣṭhatvād eṣāṃ madhurādīnām abhinirvṛtterna guṇaprakṛtīnām asaṃkhyeyatvam iti yojanā ayamarthaḥ yadyapi rasāḥ parasparasaṃsargeṇātibhūyasā yuktāḥ santo 'bhinirvṛttā dvirasādau dravye bhavanti tathāpi na teṣāṃ guṇā gurulaghvādayaḥ prakṛtayo vā madhurādīnāṃ yā yā āyuṣyatvarasābhivardhakatvādyās tā asaṃkhyeyā bhavanti kiṃtu ya eva madhurādīnāṃ pratyekaṃ guṇāḥ prakṛtayaśca uddiṣṭāsta eva miśrā bhavanti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 44]
kiṃvā guṇaprakṛtīnāmiti madhurādiṣaḍguṇasvarūpāṇām ityarthaḥ tena rasasya rasāntarasaṃsarge doṣāṇāmiva doṣāntarasaṃsarge rasānāṃ nāparisaṃkhyeyatvam ityarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 45]
prakṛtiśabdena karma vocyate tena guṇakarmaṇām ityarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 46]
madhurādīnām avāntarāsvādaviśeṣo'pi parasparasaṃsargakṛto jñeyaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 47]
yata eva heto rasānāṃ saṃsṛṣṭānāṃ nānye guṇakarmaṇī bhavataḥ ata eva saṃsṛṣṭānāṃ rasānāṃ pṛthakkarma śāstrāntare 'pi noktam ityāha tasmād ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 48]
karmaśabdeneha gauravalāghavādikārakā gurutvādayo rasaraktādijananādayaś cāpi boddhavyāḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 49]
na kevalam anyaśāstrakārai rasānāṃ saṃsṛṣṭānāṃ karma nopadiṣṭaṃ kiṃtu vayamapi nopadekṣyāma ityāha taccaivetyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 50]
taccaiva kāraṇamiti parasparasaṃsarge'pi rasānām anadhikaguṇakarmatvam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 51]
lakṣaṇena pṛthaktvaṃ lakṣaṇapṛthaktvam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 52]
tatra lakṣyate yena tallakṣaṇam atastu madhuro rasaḥ ityādinā granthena tathā snehanaprīṇanahlādana ityādinā ca yadvācyaṃ tat sarvaṃ gṛhyate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 53]
kiṃvā lakṣaṇaśabdena madhuro rasa ityādigranthavācyaṃ lakṣaṇam ucyate pṛthaktvaṃ ca rasabhedajñānārthaṃ yad vakṣyati snehanaprīṇana ityādi tad gṛhyate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 9.3 54]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 10.2}
agre tv ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 10.2 1.1]
raseṣu vācyeṣu dravyabhedam abhipretya pratipādanīyatayā parigṛhya rasānāṃ dravyajñānādhīnajñānatvād dravyābhidhānam agre kṛtam ityarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 10.2 1.2]
kiṃciditi āyurvedopayogidravyasvarūpaṃ na sarvam aprasaṅgadoṣād iti bhāvaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 10.2 2]
sarvadravyam iti kāryadravyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 10.2 3]
asminn arthe asmin prakaraṇe | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 10.2 4]
dravāntā iti vacanena pūrvoktān viṃśatiguṇān āha | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 10.2 5]
atra ca paratvāparatvādīnām ihānabhidhānena cikitsāyāṃ paratvādīnām aprādhānyaṃ darśayati ye 'pi tatrāpi yuktisaṃyogaparimāṇasaṃskārābhyāsā atyarthacikitsopayogino 'pi na te pārthivādidravyāṇāṃ śabdādivat sāṃsiddhikāḥ kiṃ tarhy ādheyāḥ ata iha naisargikaguṇakathane noktāḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 10.2 6]
uktam iti apāmārgataṇḍulīye | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 10.2 7]
etacca prādhānyāducyate tena bṛṃhaṇādyapi boddhavyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 10.2 8]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 11}
bahulaśabdo gurvādibhiḥ pratyekaṃ sambadhyate kiṃvā gandhenaiva yato gandhaguṇabahulā pṛthivyeva bhavati ata eva dravyāntaralakṣaṇe 'pi vaiśeṣikaguṇo 'nta eva paṭhyate rasaguṇabahulāni ityādi tena tatrāpi rasādibhir eva bahulaśabdo yojyaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 11 1]
sarvakāryadravyāṇāṃ pāñcabhautikatve 'pi pṛthivyādyutkarṣeṇa pārthivatvādi jñeyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 11 2]
saṃghātaḥ kāṭhinyaṃ sthairyam avicālyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 11 3]
bandhanaṃ parasparayojanaṃ prahlādaḥ śarīrendriyatarpaṇam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 11 4]
sūkṣmaṃ sūkṣmasroto'nusāri | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 11 5]
prabhā varṇaprakāśinī dīptiḥ yaduktaṃ varṇamākrāmati chāyā prabhā varṇaprakāśikā ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 11 6]
vicaraṇaṃ vicāro gatir ityarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 11 7]
sauṣiryaṃ randhrabahulatā | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 11 8]
atrākāśabāhulyaṃ dravyasya pṛthivyādibhūtāntarālpatvena bhūrivyaktākāśatvena ca jñeyaṃ yadeva bhūriśuṣiraṃ tannābhasaṃ kiṃvā ākāśaguṇabahulatvena nābhasaṃ dravyam ityucyate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 11 9]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 12}
aneneti pratiniyatadravyaguṇopadeśena yat pārthivādi dravyaṃ yadguṇaṃ tadguṇe dehe saṃpādye tad bheṣajaṃ bhavatītyarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 12 1]
tacca pārthivādi dravyaṃ na sarvathā na ca sarvasmin vyādhau bheṣajamityāha tāṃ tāṃ yuktim ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 12 2]
yuktim iti upāyam arthamiti prayojanam abhipretyeti adhikṛtya tena kenacidupāyena kvacit prayojane kiṃcid dravyamauṣadhaṃ bhavati na sarvatra | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 12 3]
tena yaducyate vairodhikānāṃ sarvadāpathyatvena nānauṣadhaṃ dravyam iti vaco virodhi tanna bhavati vairodhikāni hi saṃyogasaṃskāradeśakālādyapekṣāṇi bhavanti vairodhikasaṃyogādyabhāve tu pathyānyapi kvacit syuḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 12 4]
yānyapi sarvadāpi svabhāvādeva viṣamandakādīnyapathyāni tānyapy upāyayuktāni kvacit pathyāni bhavanti yathā udare viṣasya tilaṃ dadyāt ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 12 5]
yattu tṛṇapāṃśuprabhṛtīni nopayujyante ato na tāni bheṣajānītyucyate tanna teṣāmapi bheṣajasvedādyupāyatvena bheṣajatvāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 12 6]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 13}
pārthivādidravyāṇāṃ gurukharādiguṇayogād bheṣajatvam uktaṃ tena guṇaprabhāvādeva bheṣajaṃ syāditi śaṅkāṃ nirasyann āha na tu kevalam ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 13 1]
dravyaprabhāvād yathā dantyā virecakatvaṃ tathā maṇīnāṃ viṣādihantṛtvam ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 13 2]
guṇaprabhāvādyathā jvare tiktako rasaḥ śīte 'gnir ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 13 3]
dravyaguṇaprabhāvād yathā kṛṣṇājinasyoparīti atrāpi kṛṣṇatvaṃ guṇo'jinaṃ ca dravyamabhipretaṃ yathā vā maṇḍalair jātarūpasya tasyā eva payaḥ śṛtam tatra maṇḍalaguṇayuktasyaiva jātarūpasya kārmukatvam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 13 4]
kathaṃ kurvantītyāha tasmiṃs tasminn ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 13 5]
tāṃ tāṃ yuktimāsādyeti tāṃ tāṃ yojanāṃ prāpya | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 13 6]
yat kurvantītyādāv udāharaṇaṃ yathā śirovirecanadravyāṇi yacchirovirecanaṃ kurvanti tac chirovirecanaṃ karma yenoṣṇatvādikāraṇena śirovirecanaṃ kurvanti tadvīryaṃ vīryaṃ śaktiḥ sā ca dravyasya guṇasya vā yatra śirovirecanaṃ kurvanti tadadhikaraṇaṃ śiraḥ nānyatrādhikaraṇe śirovirecanadravyaṃ prabhavatītyarthaḥ yadeti vasantādau śirogauravādiyukte ca kāle etenākāle śīte śirovirecanaṃ stabdhatvānna kārmukaṃ kiṃtu svakāla eva yathā yena prakāreṇa pradhamanāvapīḍanādinā tathā prasāritāṅgamuttānaṃ śayane saṃstarāstṛte | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 13 7]
īṣat pralambaśirasaṃ saṃveśya cāvṛtekṣaṇam ityādinā vidhinā kurvanti sa upāyaḥ yat sādhayanti śirogauravaśūlādyuparamaṃ tat phalaṃ phalam uddeśyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 13 8]
karma kāryaṃ sādhanam uddeśyaṃ phalaṃ sādhyaṃ yathā yāganiṣpādyo dharmaḥ kāryatayā karma tajjanyastu svargādir uddeśyaḥ phalam evaṃ vamanādiṣvapi karmādhikaraṇādyunneyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 13 9]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 14}
samprati dravyam abhidhāya vikṛtānāṃ rasānām eva bhedam āha bhedaś caiṣām ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 14 1]
prabhāvaśabdo dravyadeśakālaiḥ pratyekaṃ yujyate tatra dravyaprabhāvād yathā somaguṇātirekān madhuraḥ ityādi deśaprabhāvād yathā himavati drākṣādāḍimādīni madhurāṇi bhavantyanyatrāmlānītyādi kālaprabhāvādyathā bālāmraṃ sakaṣāyaṃ taruṇamamlaṃ pakvaṃ madhuraṃ tathā hemante oṣadhyo madhurā varṣāsv amlā ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 14 2]
agnisaṃyogādayo ye 'nye rasahetavas te 'pi kāle dravye vāntarbhāvanīyāḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 14 3]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 15.2}
bhedamāha svādur ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 15.2 1]
tatra svādoramlādiyogāt pañca śeṣair iti āditvenopayuktād anyaiḥ tenāmlasya lavaṇādiyogāc catvāri evaṃ lavaṇasya kaṭvādiyogāt trīṇi kaṭukasya tiktakaṣāyayogād dve tiktasya kaṣāyayogād ekam evaṃ pañcadaśa dvirasāni | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 15.2 2]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 17.1}
trirasam āha pṛthag ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 17.1 1]
madhurasyāmlādirasacatuṣṭayena pṛthag ityekaikaśo yuktasya śeṣairlavaṇādibhir yogo bhavati tatra madhurasyāmlayuktasya śeṣalavaṇādiyogāc catvāri tathā madhurasya lavaṇayuktasya kaṭvādiyogāt trīṇi tathā kaṭuyuktasya tiktādiyogād dve tathā tiktayuktasya kaṣāyayogād ekam evaṃ madhureṇādisthitena daśa | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 17.1 2]
evamamlasyādisthitasya lavaṇayuktasya kaṭvādiyogāt trīṇi tathā kaṭukayuktasya śeṣābhyāṃ yogād dve evaṃ tiktayuktasya kaṣāyayogād ekam evam amlasya ṣaṭ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 17.1 3]
anenaiva nyāyena lavaṇasya trīṇi kaṭoś caikameva evaṃ militvā trirasāni viṃśatiḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 17.1 4]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 21.1}
catūrase svādvamlāv ādisthitau lavaṇādibhir ekaikaśyena yuktau śeṣaiḥ kaṭvādibhir yogāt ṣaḍ bhavanti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 21.1 1]
svādulavaṇau sahitau ādisthitau kaṭvādibhiriti kaṭutiktābhyāṃ pṛthagyuktau śeṣair iti tiktakaṣāyābhyāṃ teneha bahuvacanaṃ jātau boddhavyam evaṃ trīṇi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 21.1 2]
svādūṣaṇau tathetyanena svādukaṭukatiktakaṣāyarūpam ekam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 21.1 3]
kaṭvādyair ityādāv api bahuvacanaṃ jātau | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 21.1 4]
amlalavaṇau saṃyuktau kaṭunā sahitau śeṣābhyāṃ yogād dve tathāmlalavaṇau tiktayuktau śeṣayogād ekam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 21.1 5]
amlakaṭū tathetyanenāmlakaṭutiktakaṣāyarūpam ekam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 21.1 6]
yujyete tv ityādinā caikam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 21.1 7]
evaṃ pañcadaśa catūrasāni | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 21.1 8]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 22.1}
apavarjanāditi tyāgāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 22.1 1]
atra ca rasānāṃ guṇatvenaikasmin dravye samavāyo yogaśabdenocyate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 22.1 2]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 23.2}
rasasaṃsargasya prakārāntareṇāsaṃkhyeyatām āha triṣaṣṭiḥ syād ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 23.2 1]
anuraso'gre vakṣyamāṇaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 23.2 2]
atra ca triṣaṣṭyātmakarase rasānurasakalpanā nāsti kevale madhurādau tadabhāvāt tena yathāsambhavaṃ saptapañcāśatsaṃyogaviṣayaṃ rasānurasakalpanaṃ jñeyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 23.2 3]
kiṃvā ekarase'pyanuraso'styevāvyapadeśyaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 23.2 4]
prakārāntareṇāpy asaṃkhyeyatām āha rasās taratamābhyām ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 23.2 5]
madhuramadhurataramadhuratamādibhedād asaṃkhyeyatā rasānāṃ bhavatīti bhāvaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 23.2 6]
kiṃvā rasānurasatvenaiva yāsaṃkhyeyatā tatraivāyaṃ hetuḥ rasās taratamābhyāmityādiḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 23.2 7]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 24.2}
evamasaṃkhyeyatve'pi triṣaṣṭividhaiva kalpanā cikitsāvyavahārārtham ihācāryaiḥ kalpitetyāha saṃyogā ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 24.2 1]
tatra yogyatvād iti tatra svasthāturahitacikitsāprayoge 'natisaṃkṣepavistararūpatayā hitatvād ityarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 24.2 2]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 26.2}
tameva cikitsāprayogam āha kvacidityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 26.2 1]
atrādigrahaṇād deśakālabalādīnām anuktānāṃ grahaṇam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 26.2 2]
etadeva saṃyuktāsaṃyuktarasakalpanaṃ bhinnarasadravyamelakād vānekarasaikadravyaprayogād ekarasadravyaprayogādvā bhavatīti darśayannāha dravyāṇītyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 26.2 3]
dvirasādīni utpattisiddhadvirasatrirasādīni dvirasaṃ yathā kaṣāyamadhuro mudgaḥ trirasaṃ yathā madhurāmlakaṣāyaṃ ca viṣṭambhi guru śītalam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 26.2 4]
pittaśleṣmaharaṃ bhavyam ityādi catūrasas tilaḥ yad uktaṃ snigdhoṣṇamadhuras tiktaḥ kaṣāyaḥ kaṭukas tilaḥ pañcarasaṃ tv āmalakaṃ harītakī ca śivā pañcarasā ityādivacanāt vyaktaṣaḍrasaṃ tu dravyam ihānuktaṃ viṣaṃ tv avyaktaṣaḍrasasaṃyuktaṃ hārīte tv eṇamāṃsaṃ vyaktaṣaḍrasasaṃyuktam uktam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 26.2 5]
evaṃ dvirasādidravyayogād dvirasādyupayogaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 26.2 6]
tathā saṃyuktāṃśca rasāniti ekaikarasādidravyamelakāt saṃyuktān rasān ekaikaśaḥ kalpayanti prayojayanti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 26.2 7]
gadān pratīti prādhānyena tena svasthavṛtte 'pi boddhavyaṃ kiṃvā dvirasādibhedo gada eva svasthe tu sarvarasaprayoga eva yaduktaṃ samasarvarasaṃ sātmyaṃ samadhātoḥ praśasyate iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 26.2 8]
evaṃ ca vyākhyāne sati kvacideko rasa ityādinā samamasya na paunaruktyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 26.2 9]
kiṃvā kvacid eko rasaḥ ityādinā svamatam uktam atraivārthe dravyāṇi dvirasādīni ityādinācāryāntarasammatiṃ darśayati ata evānyācāryāntarābhiprāyeṇa kalpayantītyuktaṃ tena na paunaruktyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 26.2 10]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 27.2}
rasajñānaphalamāha yaḥ syād ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 27.2 1]
atra rasavikalpajñānādeva vyādhihetudravyajñānaṃ kṛtsnamavaruddhaṃ rasajñānenaiva prāyaḥ sakaladravyaguṇasya vakṣyamāṇatvāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 27.2 2]
doṣavikalpajñānācca liṅgajñānaṃ yāvaddhi liṅgaṃ tat sarvaṃ doṣavikalpasambaddham | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 27.2 3]
rasadoṣavikalpajñānāt tu bheṣajajñānaṃ yato rasataḥ svarūpajñānaṃ bheṣajadravyasya doṣataśca bheṣajaprayogaviṣayavijñānam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 27.2 4]
kiṃvā rasavikalpāc ca tathā doṣavikalpāc ca hetvādijñānaṃ pṛthageva vaktavyaṃ rasabhedāddhi tatkāryaṃ liṅgamapi jñāyate hetubheṣajavijñānaṃ tu | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 27.2 5]
rasabhedavijñānādeva vaktavyaṃ yato rasabhedavad dravyameva vikārāṇāṃ heturbheṣajaṃ ca bhavatīti evaṃ doṣabhedaṃ jñātvā ca tasya samānaṃ hetuṃ pratyeti doṣavirodhi ca dravyaṃ bheṣajamiti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 27.2 6]
tad yuktam uktaṃ na sa muhyedvikārāṇāṃ hetuliṅgopaśāntiṣviti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 27.2 7]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 28.2}
pūrvoktarasānurasalakṣaṇamāha vyakta ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 28.2 1]
śuṣkasya ceti cakārād ārdrasya ca ādau ceti cakārādante ca tena śuṣkasya vārdrasya vā prathamajihvāsambandhe vāsvādānte vā yo vyaktatvena madhuro 'yam amlo 'yam ityādinā vikalpena gṛhyate sa vyaktaḥ yas tūktāvasthācatuṣṭaye 'pi vyakto nopalabhyate kiṃ tarhy avyapadeśyatayā chāyāmātreṇa kāryadarśanena vā mīyate so 'nurasa iti vākyārthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 28.2 2]
yataśca madhurādaya eva vyaktatvāvyaktatvābhyāṃ rasānurasarūpāḥ ato'vyakto nāma saptamo raso nāsti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 28.2 3]
ayaṃ cārthaḥ pūrvaṃ pratiṣiddho 'pyanuguṇaspaṣṭahetuprāptyā punar niṣidhyate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 28.2 4]
anye tv āhuḥ śuṣkasya cetyanena yasya dravyasya śuṣkasya cārdrasya copayogaḥ tatra śuṣkāvasthāyāṃ yo 'vyaktaḥ sa rasa ucyate yastvārdrāvasthāyāṃ vyaktaḥ san śuṣkāvasthāyāṃ nānuyāti nāsau rasaḥ kiṃtv anurasaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 28.2 5]
yathā pippalyā ārdrāyā madhuro raso vyaktaḥ śuṣkāyāstu pippalyāḥ kaṭukaḥ tena kaṭuka eva rasaḥ pippalyāḥ madhurastvanurasaḥ yastu drākṣādīnām ārdrāvasthāyāṃ śuṣkāvasthāyāṃ ca madhura eva tatra vipratipattirapi nāsti tena tatra madhura eva rasaḥ nityārdraprayojyānāṃ tu kāñjikatakrādīnāmādau vyakto ya upalabhyate rasaḥ anu copalabhyate yaḥ so 'nuraso yuktas tiktatvādiḥ tathā ārdrāvasthāyāṃ śuṣkāvasthāviparīto yaḥ pippalyā iva madhuraḥ so 'nurasa iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 28.2 6]
kiṃtv ārdrāpi pippalī madhurarasaiveti paśyāmaḥ yato vakṣyati śleṣmalā madhurā cārdrā gurvī snigdhā ca pippalī iti madhurasya tatrānurasatve gurutvaśleṣmakartṛtvāny anupapannāni tena ārdrā pippalī vyaktamadhurarasaiva śuṣkā tu madhurānuraseti yuktam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 28.2 7]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2}
samprati pūrvoktagurvādiguṇātiriktān paratvāparatvādīn daśa guṇān rasadharmatvenopadeṣṭavyān āha paretyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2 1]
tacca paratvaṃ pradhānatvam aparatvam apradhānatvam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2 2]
tadvivaraṇaṃ deśakāletyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2 3]
tatra deśo maruḥ paraḥ anūpo 'paraḥ kālo visargaḥ paraḥ ādānamaparaḥ vayastaruṇaṃ param aparam itaran mānaṃ ca śarīrasya yathā vakṣyamāṇaṃ śarīre paraṃ tato'nyadaparaṃ pākavīryarasāstu ye yasya yoginaste taṃ prati parāḥ ayaugikās tv aparāḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2 4]
ādigrahaṇāt prakṛtibalādīnāṃ grahaṇam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2 5]
kiṃvā paratvāparatve vaiśeṣikokte jñeye tatra deśāpekṣayā saṃnikṛṣṭadeśasambandhinam apekṣya vidūradeśasambandhini paratvaṃ saṃnikṛṣṭadeśasambandhini cāparatvaṃ bhavati evaṃ saṃnikṛṣṭaviprakṛṣṭakālāpekṣayā ca sthavire paratvaṃ yūni cāparatvaṃ bhavati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2 6]
vayaḥprabhṛtiṣu paratvāparatvaṃ yathāsambhavaṃ kāladeśakṛtam evehopayogād upacaritam apyabhihitaṃ yato na guṇe mānādau guṇāntarasambhavaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2 7]
yuktiścetyādau yojanā doṣādyapekṣayā bheṣajasya samīcīnakalpanā ata evoktaṃ yā tu yujyate yā kalpanā yaugikī bhavati sā tu yuktir ucyate ayaugikī tu kalpanāpi satī yuktir nocyate putro 'pyaputravat | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2 8]
yuktiśceyaṃ saṃyogaparimāṇasaṃskārādyantargatāpy atyupayuktatvāt pṛthagucyate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2 9]
saṃkhyāṃ lakṣayati saṃkhyetyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2 10]
gaṇitam ihaikadvitryādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2 11]
saṃyogamāha yoga ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2 12]
saheti militānāṃ dravyāṇāṃ yogaḥ prāptirityarthaḥ sahetyanenehākiṃcitkaraṃ parasparasaṃyogaṃ nirākaroti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2 13]
tadbhedamāha dvaṃdvetyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2 14]
tatra dvaṃdvakarmajo yathā yudhyamānayor meṣayoḥ sarvakarmajo yathā bhāṇḍe prakṣipyamāṇānāṃ māṣāṇāṃ bahulamāṣakriyā yogajaḥ ekakarmajo yathā vṛkṣavāyasayoḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2 15]
anitya iti saṃyogasya karmajatvenānityatvaṃ darśayati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2 16]
vibhāgamāha vibhāgas tv ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2 17]
vibhaktiḥ vibhajanam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2 18]
vibhaktimeva vivṛṇoti viyoga iti saṃyogasya vigamo viyogaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2 19]
tat kiṃ saṃyogābhāva eva viyoga ityāha bhāgaśo graha iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2 20]
vibhāgaśo vibhaktatvena grahaṇaṃ yato bhavatīti bhāvaḥ tena vibhaktirityeṣā bhāvarūpā pratītir na saṃyogābhāvamātraṃ bhavati kiṃtarhi bhāvarūpavibhāgaguṇayuktā ityarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2 21]
pṛthaktvaṃ tu idaṃ dravyaṃ paṭalakṣaṇaṃ ghaṭāt pṛthag ityādikā buddhiryato bhavati tat pṛthaktvaṃ bhavati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2 22]
taccācāryas traividhyenāha pṛthaktvamityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2 23]
tatra yat sarvathāsaṃyujyamānayoriva meruhimācalayoḥ pṛthaktvam etadasaṃyoga ityanenoktam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2 24]
tathā saṃyujyamānānāmapi pṛthaktvaṃ vijātīyānāṃ mahiṣavarāhādīnāṃ tadāha vailakṣaṇyamityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2 25]
viśiṣṭalakṣaṇayuktatvalakṣitaṃ vijātīyānāṃ pṛthaktvam ityarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2 26]
tathaikajātīyānāmapy avilakṣaṇānāṃ māṣāṇāṃ pṛthaktvaṃ bhavatītyāha anekateti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2 27]
ekajātīyeṣu hi saṃyukteṣu na vailakṣaṇyaṃ nāpyasaṃyogaḥ atha cānekatā pṛthaktvarūpā bhavatīti bhāvaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2 28]
kiṃvā pṛthaktvaṃ guṇāntaramicchan lokavyavahārārtham asaṃyogavailakṣaṇyānekatārūpameva yathodāhṛtaṃ pṛthaktvaṃ darśayati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2 29]
mānaṃ prasthāḍhakāditulādimeyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2 30.1]
karaṇaṃ guṇāntarādhāyakatvaṃ saṃskaraṇamityarthaḥ yadvakṣyati saṃskāro hi guṇāntarādhānamucyate iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2 30.2]
bhāvasya ṣaṣṭikādervyāyāmādeś cābhyasanam abhyāsaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2 31]
abhyasanameva lokaprasiddhābhyāṃ paryāyābhyāṃ vivṛṇoti śīlanaṃ satatakriyeti yaṃ lokāḥ śīlanasatatakriyābhyām abhidadhati so 'bhyāsa iti bhāvaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2 32]
ayaṃ ca saṃyogasaṃskāraviśeṣarūpo 'pi viśeṣeṇa cikitsopayuktatvāt pṛthagucyate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2 33]
na yathāvat pravartata iti vacanena śabdādiṣu ca gurvādiṣu ca parādīnāmaprādhānyaṃ sūcayati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 35.2 34]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 36.2}
samprati rasānāṃ parasparasaṃyogo guṇa uktaḥ tathāgre ca snigdhatvādirguṇo vācyaḥ sa ca guṇarūparase na sambhavatīti yathā rasānāṃ guṇanirdeśo boddhavyas tadāha guṇā ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 36.2 1]
guṇā guṇāśrayā noktā iti dīrghaṃjīvitīye samavāyī tu niśceṣṭaḥ kāraṇaṃ guṇaḥ ityanena | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 36.2 2]
rasaguṇāniti rase snigdhādīn guṇān nirdiṣṭān tad rasādhāradravyaguṇān eva vidyāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 36.2 3]
nanu yadi dravyaguṇā eva te tat kimiti rasaguṇatvenocyanta ityāha karturityādi karturiti tantrakartuḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 36.2 4]
abhiprāyā iti tatra tatropacāreṇa tathā sāmānyaśabdādiprayogeṇa tantrakaraṇabuddhayaḥ sāmānyaśabdopacārādiprayogaś ca prakaraṇādivaśād eva sphuṭatvāt tathā prayojanavaśāc ca kriyate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 36.2 5]
tacca prakaraṇādi ataśca prakṛtaṃ buddhvā ityādau darśayiṣyāmaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 36.2 6]
iha ca dravyaguṇānāṃ raseṣu yadupacaraṇaṃ tasyāyamabhiprāyo yat madhurādinirdeśenaiva snigdhaśītādiguṇā api prāyo madhurādyavyabhicāriṇo dravye nirdiṣṭā bhavantīti na madhuratvaṃ nirdiśya snigdhatvādipratipādanaṃ punaḥ pṛthak kriyata iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 36.2 7]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 37.2}
abhiprāyapṛthaktve sati yathā grantho boddhavyas tadāha ataś cetyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 37.2 1]
tatra prakṛtaṃ buddhvā yathā kṣārāḥ kṣīraṃ phalaṃ puṣpam ityatrodbhidagaṇasya prakṛtatvāt kṣīramiti snuhyādikṣīram eva kṣīraśabdena vadet | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 37.2 2]
deśāntaraṃ buddhveti yathā śirasi śodhane 'bhidhīyamāne krimivyādhau iti tacchirogatakrimivyādhāv eva bhavati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 37.2 3]
kālāntare yathā vamanakāle 'bhihitaṃ pratigrahāṃś copahārayed iti tatra pratigrahaśabdena pātramucyate na tu grahaṇaṃ pratigrahaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 37.2 4]
tantrakartur abhiprāyān iti yathoktaṃ raseṣu guṇāropaṇe tad boddhavyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 37.2 5]
upāyān iti śāstropāyān tantrayuktirūpān | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 37.2 6]
artham abhidheyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 37.2 7]
yadyapi prakṛtādayo 'pi tantrakartur abhiprāyā eva tathāpi yatra prakṛtatvādi na sphuṭaṃ pratīyate tatra tantrakartur abhiprāyatvena boddhavyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 37.2 8]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 38.2}
ṣaḍvibhaktīr iti madhurādiṣaḍvibhāgān ityarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 38.2 1]
ṣaṭ pañcabhūtaprabhavā iti pañcabhūtaprabhavāḥ santo yathoktena prakāreṇa somaguṇātirekāt ityādinā yathā ṣaṭ saṃkhyātāḥ ṣaṭsaṃkhyāparicchinnā bhavanti tathā vakṣyāmīti yojanā | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 38.2 2]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 39}
samprati rasānām ādikāraṇameva tāvad āha saumyā ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 39 1]
saumyāḥ somadevatākāḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 39 2]
bhraśyamānā iti vadatā bhūmisambandhavyatirekeṇāntarīkṣeritaiḥ pṛthivyādiparamāṇvādibhiḥ sambandho rasārambhako bhavatīti darśyate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 39 3]
mūrtīr iti vyaktīḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 39 4]
abhiprīṇayantīti tarpayanti kiṃvā janayanti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 39 5]
abhimūrchanti rasā iti vyaktiṃ yānti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 39 6]
atra cāntarīkṣamudakaṃ rasakāraṇatve pradhānatvāduktaṃ tena kṣitistham api sthāvarajaṅgamotpattau rasakāraṇaṃ bhavatyeva | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 39 7]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 40.2}
somaguṇātirekāditi atirekaśabdena sarveṣveva raseṣu sarvabhūtasāṃnidhyam asti kvacit tu kasyacid bhūtaguṇasyātirekād rasaviśeṣe bhavatīti darśayati etacca madhuraṃ prati abguṇātiriktatvaṃ viśeṣotpattau kāraṇatvena jñeyaṃ yaccādhārakāraṇatvam apāṃ tat sarvasādhāraṇam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 40.2 1]
evaṃ lavaṇe 'py apāṃ kāraṇatvaṃ jñeyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 40.2 2]
lavaṇastu suśrute pṛthivyagnyatirekāt paṭhitaḥ asmiṃś ca virodhe kāryavirodho nāstyeva | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 40.2 3]
nanu uṣṇaśītābhyāmagnisalilābhyāṃ kṛtasya lavaṇasyāpy uṣṇaśītatvena bhavitavyaṃ tal lavaṇaṃ katham uṣṇaṃ bhavati naivaṃ yato bhūtānām ayaṃ svabhāvo yat kenacit prakāreṇa saṃniviṣṭāḥ kaṃcid guṇam ārabhante na sarvam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 40.2 4]
yathā makuṣṭhake 'dbhir madhuro rasaḥ kriyate na snehaḥ tathā saindhave vahnināpi noṣṇatvam ārabhyate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 40.2 5]
ayaṃ ca bhūtānāṃ saṃniveśo 'dṛṣṭaprabhāvakṛta eva sa ca saṃniveśaḥ kāryadarśanenonneyaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 40.2 6]
tena yatra kāryaṃ dṛśyate tatra kalpyate yathā lavaṇe uṣṇatvād agnir viṣyanditvācca jalamanumīyate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 40.2 7.1]
āgamavedanīyaścāyamartho nātrāsmadvidhānāṃ kalpanāḥ prasaranti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 40.2 8]
etena yaducyate toyavat pṛthivyādayo'pi kimiti pṛthagrasāntaraṃ na kurvanti tathā toyavātādisaṃyogādibhyaḥ kimiti rasāntarāṇi notpadyanta iti tadapi bhūtasvabhāvāparyanuyogād eva pratyuktam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 40.2 9]
iha ca kāraṇatvaṃ bhūtānāṃ rasasya madhuratvādiviśeṣa eva nimittakāraṇarūpam ucyate tena nīrasānām api hi dahanādīnāṃ kāraṇatvamupapannam eva vyutpāditam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 40.2 10]
rasabhedaṃ dṛṣṭāntena sādhayannāha evam ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 40.2 11]
rasānāṃ ṣaṭtvaṃ mahābhūtānāṃ nyūnātirekaviśeṣāt somaguṇātirekapṛthivyagnyatirekādeḥ ṣaḍutpādakāraṇādupapannaṃ ṣaḍbhyaḥ kāraṇebhyaḥ ṣaṭ kāryāṇi bhavantīti yuktameveti bhāvaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 40.2 12]
bhūtānāṃ yathā nānāvarṇākṛtiviśeṣā mahābhūtānāṃ nyūnātirekaviśeṣāt tathā rasānām apīti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 40.2 13]
bhūtānāṃ yathoktānām atirekaviśeṣahetum āha ṣaḍṛtukatvād ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 40.2 14]
ṣaḍṛtukatvena kālo nānāhemantādirūpatayā kaṃcidbhūtaviśeṣaṃ kvacidvardhayati sa cātmakāryaṃ rasaṃ puṣṭaṃ karoti yathā hemantakāle somaguṇātireko bhavati śiśire vāyvākāśātirekaḥ evaṃ tasyāśitīyoktarasotpādakrameṇa vasantādāv api bhūtotkarṣo jñeyaḥ ṣaḍṛtukācceti cakāreṇāhorātrakṛto 'pi bhūtotkarṣo jñeyaḥ tathādṛṣṭakṛtaś ca tena hemantādāv api rasāntarotpādaḥ kvacidvastuny upapanno bhavati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 40.2 15]
yadyapi ca ṛtubhede'pi bhūtotkarṣaviśeṣa eva kāraṇaṃ yaduktaṃ tāv etāv arkavāyū ityādi tathāpi bījāṅkurakāryakāraṇabhāvavat saṃsārānāditayaiva bhūtaviśeṣartvoḥ kāryakāraṇabhāvo vācyaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 40.2 16]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 41}
bhūtaviśeṣakṛtaṃ rasānāṃ dharmāntaram āha tatretyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 41 1]
prāyeṇeti na sarve | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 41 2]
rasā iti rasayuktāni dravyāṇi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 41 3]
plavanatvāditi gatimattvāt yadyapi gatiradho'pi syāt tathāpi laghutvaparigatagatir iha vāyor ūrdhvam eva gamanaṃ karoti yathā śālmalītulānām | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 41 4]
hetvantaram āha ūrdhvajvalanatvāc cāgneriti agner apyūrdhvagatitvād ityarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 41 5]
nimnagatvamadhogatvameva | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 41 6]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 42}
yathādravyamiti yadyasya rasasya dravyam ādhāras tadanatikrameṇa | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 42 1]
etena rasānāṃ guṇakarmaṇī rasādhāre dravye boddhavye iti darśayati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 42 2]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 43.2}
tatretyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 43.2 1]
madhura ādāv ucyate praśastāyuṣyādiguṇatayā prāyaḥ prāṇipriyatayā ca | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 43.2 2]
ṣaḍindriyāṇi manasā samam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 43.2 3]
jīvanaḥ abhighātādimūrchitasya jīvanaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 43.2 4]
āyuṣyastu āyuḥprakarṣakāritvena | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 43.2 5]
kṣīṇasya saṃdhānakaro dhātupoṣakatvena kiṃvā kṣīṇaścāsau kṣataśceti tena kṣīṇakṣatasya uraḥkṣataṃ saṃdadhāti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 43.2 6]
ṣaṭpadādyabhīṣṭatvaguṇakathanaṃ prameharūpādijñānopayuktam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 43.2 7]
yaduktaṃ mūtre 'bhidhāvanti pipīlikāśca iti tathā riṣṭe vakṣyati yasmin gṛdhnanti makṣikāḥ iti anena ca madhuratvaṃ jñāyate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 43.2 8]
akṣyāmayenaivābhiṣyande labdhe viśeṣopādānārthaṃ punarvacanaṃ kiṃvā abhiṣyando nāsādiṣvapi jñeyaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 43.2 9]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 43.3}
hṛdayaṃ tarpayatīti hṛdyo bhavati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 43.3 1]
bhuktam apakarṣayatīti sārayati kledayati tathā jarayati bhuktameva | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 43.3 2]
avamūtritaṃ mūtraviṣairjantubhiḥ parisarpitaṃ ca sparśaviśeṣaiḥ kāraṇḍādibhiḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 43.3 3]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 43.4}
vikāsī kledachedanaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 43.4 1]
adhaḥsraṃsī viṣyandanaśīlaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 43.4 2]
sarvarasapratyanīkabhūta iti yatra mātrātirikto lavaṇo bhavati tatra nānyo rasa upalakṣyate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 43.4 3]
āhārayogīti āhāre sadā yujyate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 43.4 4]
mohayati vaicittyaṃ kurute | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 43.4 5]
mūrchayatīti saṃjñānāśaṃ karoti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 43.4 6]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 43.7}
vipākasya prabhāvo vipākaprabhāvaḥ vipākaśca kaṭūnāṃ kaṭureva rasasya vīryasya ca prabhāvo rasavīryaprabhāvaḥ ayaṃ ca vakṣyamāṇe sarvatra hetuḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 43.7 1]
caraṇādīnāṃ sākṣādgrahaṇaṃ tatraiva prāyo vātavikārabhāvāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 43.7 2]
atra ca vipākaprabhāvādikathanam udāharaṇārthaṃ tena madhurādiṣu vipākādikāryam unneyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 43.7 3]
glapayati harṣakṣayaṃ karoti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 43.7 4]
pīḍano vraṇapīḍanaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 43.7 5]
śarīrakledasyopayokteti ācūṣakaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 43.7 6]
śīto'laghuśca ityakārapraśleṣād alaghuḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 43.7 7]
avagṛhṇātīti baddhāni karoti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 43.7 8]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 44}
pṛthaktveneti ekaikaśo mātraśaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 44 1]
ekatveneti ekīkṛtya samudāyamātraśa ityarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 44 2]
mātraśa iti mātrayā | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Sū., 26, 44 3]
