katiprakāraḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 15.2 1]
katidheti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 15.2 1.1]
puruṣa ityanena cāviśeṣeṇa puruṣaśabdābhidheyo 'rtho 'bhidhīyate yataḥ khādayaścetanāṣaṣṭhā ityādinā tathā caturviṃśatikabhedabhinnaśca karmapuruṣa eva śarīrī vācyaḥ tathā cetanādhāturapyekaḥ smṛtaḥ puruṣasaṃjñakaḥ ityanenātmaiva śarīrarahitaḥ puruṣaśabdārthatvena vācyaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 15.2 2]
puruṣadhāraṇāddhātuḥ tena dhātubhedeneti puruṣadhāraṇārthabhedena | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 15.2 3]
dhīmanniti viśeṣaṇena ya eva dhīmān sa eva puruṣabhedādikam imaṃ vakṣyamāṇaṃ susūkṣmaṃ vaktuṃ samartha iti darśayati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 15.2 4]
puruṣaḥ kāraṇaṃ kasmād iti kasmāddhetoḥ puruṣaḥ saṃsāre pradhānaṃ sthāyikāraṇam ityarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 15.2 5]
prabhavatyasmād iti prabhavaḥ kāraṇam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 15.2 6]
yoniṣviti jātiṣu | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 15.2 7]
sarvā iti parapuruṣagatā api | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 15.2 8]
kṣetrajñaḥ ātmā | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 15.2 9]
kṣetram avyaktavarjitaṃ sarvaṃ vakṣyamāṇam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 15.2 10]
jñeyamityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 15.2 11]
asati kṣetre kṣetrajñānābhāvānna kṣetrajñatvamupapadyate iti bhāvaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 15.2 12]
sākṣibhūta iti sākṣisadṛśaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 15.2 13]
viśeṣo vedanākṛta iti putrādijñānarūpavedanājanito harṣādiviśeṣa ityarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 15.2 14]
tisṛṇāmiti atītānāgatavartamānānāṃ duḥkharūpāṇāṃ madhye kāṃ cikitsati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 15.2 15]
atītāmityādau kiṃśabdo'dhyāhāryaḥ tena kim atītāṃ cikitsati kiṃ vartamānāṃ kiṃvā bhaviṣyatīmiti yojyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 15.2 16]
sthānaṃ nāstīti kṣaṇikatvena cikitsāyāḥ pravṛttiyogyakālāvasthānaṃ nāsti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 15.2 17]
vedanānāṃ kāraṇam adhiṣṭhānaṃ ca yadyapi dīrghaṃjīvitīye 'pyuktaṃ tathāpīha prakaraṇavaśād viśeṣapratītyākāṅkṣayā ca viśiṣṭaḥ punaḥ praśnāḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 15.2 18]
praśnārthāścāmī uttaragranthe ācāryeṇa prapañcanīyā iti neha vyākaraṇīyāḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 15.2 19]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 16.2}
khādaya ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 16.2 1.1]
khādayaḥ khaṃ vāyur agnir āpaḥ kṣitistathā iti vakṣyamāṇāḥ cetanāṣaṣṭhā ityatra cetanāśabdena cetanādhāraḥ samanaskaṃ ātmā gṛhyate khādigrahaṇena cendriyāṇi khādimayānyavaruddhāni | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 16.2 2]
ayaṃ ca vaiśeṣikadarśanaparigṛhītaś cikitsāśāstraviṣayaḥ puruṣaḥ ayameva pañcamahābhūtaśarīrisamavāyaḥ puruṣaḥ ityanena suśrutenāpyuktaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 16.2 3]
smṛta iti bhāṣayā pūrvācāryāṇām apyayaṃ puruṣaśabdavācyo'bhipreto nāsmatkalpita iti darśayati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 16.2 4]
puri śarīre śete iti vyutpattyā ya ātmā puruṣaśabdenocyate tamāha cetanetyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 16.2 5]
atra puruṣa iti kartavye yat puruṣasaṃjñaka iti karoti tena na cetanādhāturūpaḥ puruṣaścikitsāyam abhipretaḥ kiṃtu śāstrāntaravyavahārānurodhād ihāpyayaṃ puruṣaśabdena saṃjñita iti darśayati cikitsāviṣayastu ṣaḍdhātuka eva puruṣaḥ ata eva tatra saṃjñitagrahaṇaṃ na kṛtam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 16.2 6]
ayaṃ ca puruṣaśabdo gavādāvapi ṣaḍdhātusamudāye yadyapi vartate tathāpi sarvapradhāne nara eva viśeṣeṇa vartate tena nātiprasiddhe gavādau puruṣaśabdaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 16.2 7]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 17.2}
ṣaḍdhāturūpameva puruṣaṃ punaḥ sāṃkhyadarśanabhedāc caturviṃśatikabhedenāha punaścetyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 17.2 1]
caturviṃśatikameva vibhajate mana ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 17.2 2]
yadyapi pañcaviṃśatitattvamayo'yaṃ puruṣaḥ sāṃkhyairucyate yadāha mūlaprakṛtiravikṛtirmahadādyāḥ prakṛtivikṛtayaḥ sapta | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 17.2 3.1]
ṣoḍaśakastu vikāro na prakṛtir na vikṛtiḥ puruṣaḥ iti tathāpīha prakṛtivyatiriktaṃ codāsīnaṃ puruṣamavyaktatvasādharmyād avyaktāyāṃ prakṛtāveva prakṣipya avyaktaśabdenaiva gṛhṇāti tena caturviṃśatikaḥ puruṣaḥ ityaviruddham | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 17.2 3.2]
udāsīnasya hi sūkṣmasya bhedapratipādanam ihānatiprayojanam iti na kṛtam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 17.2 4]
daśendriyāṇīti pañca karmendriyāṇi pañca buddhīndriyāṇi ca | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 17.2 5]
aṣṭadhātukīti khādipañcakabuddhyavyaktāhaṃkārarūpā vakṣyati hi khādīni buddhiravyaktam ahaṅkārastathāṣṭamaḥ iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 17.2 6]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 19.2}
atra caturviṃśatike prathamoddiṣṭaṃ mano lakṣayitumāha lakṣaṇam ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 19.2 1]
yathā jñānasyābhāvo jñānasya bhāvaśca manogamako bhavati tadāha satītyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 19.2 2]
vaivṛttyānmanasa iti indriyeṇāsaṃyogāt sānnidhyāditi indriyeṇa manasaḥ saṃbandhāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 19.2 3]
evaṃ manyate yadā yugapad indriyārthā indriyaiḥ saṃyujyante tadā kvacid indriyārthe jñānaṃ bhavati kvacinna bhavatīti dṛṣṭaṃ tenemau jñānabhāvābhāvau jñānakāraṇāntaraṃ darśayataḥ yacca tat kāraṇāntaraṃ tanmanaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 19.2 4]
tacca kāraṇaṃ manorūpaṃ yadyātmavadyugapat sarvendriyavyāpakaṃ svīkriyate kiṃvā anekasaṃkhyam indriyavat svīkriyate tadā punarapi yugapad indriyārthasaṃbandhe pañcabhir jñānair bhavitavyaṃ vibhunā vā manasā anekair vā manobhir yugapad adhiṣṭhitatvād indriyāṇāṃ na ca bhavanti yugapajjñānāni tasmādyugapajjñānānudayāl liṅgānmano'ṇurūpamekaṃ ca sidhyatītyāha aṇutvamityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 19.2 5]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 21.2}
manoguṇamabhidhāya manoviṣayamāha cintyamityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 21.2 1]
cintyaṃ kartavyatayā akartavyatayā vā yanmanasā cintyate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 21.2 2]
vicāryam upapattyanupapattibhyāṃ yadvimṛśyate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 21.2 3]
ūhyaṃ ca yat sambhāvanayā ūhyate evametadbhaviṣyati iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 21.2 4]
dhyeyaṃ bhāvanājñānaviṣayam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 21.2 5]
saṃkalpyaṃ guṇavattayā doṣavattayā vāvadhāraṇāviṣayam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 21.2 6]
yat kiṃcidityanena sukhādyanuktaviṣayāvarodhaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 21.2 7]
manaso jñeyamiti indriyanirapekṣamanogrāhyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 21.2 8]
ete ca mano'rthāḥ śabdādirūpā eva tena ṣaṣṭhārthakalpanayā na caturviṃśatisaṃkhyātirekaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 21.2 9]
sukhādayas tu śabdādivyatiriktā mano'rthā buddhibhedagrahaṇenaiva grāhyāḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 21.2 10]
manoviṣayamabhidhāya manaḥkarmāha indriyetyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 21.2 11]
indriyābhigrahaḥ indriyādhiṣṭhānaṃ manasaḥ karma tathā svasya nigraho manasaḥ karma mano hy aniṣṭaviṣayaprasṛtaṃ manasaiva niyamyate manaśca guṇāntarayuktaṃ sadviṣayāntarān niyamayati ityāhureke | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 21.2 12]
yaduktam viṣayapravaṇaṃ cittaṃ dhṛtibhraṃśānna śakyate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 21.2 13]
niyantum ahitād arthād dhṛtirhi niyamātmikā iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 21.2 14]
tena dhṛtyā kāraṇabhūtayā ātmānaṃ niyamayatīti na svātmani kriyāvirodhaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 21.2 15]
manaḥkarmāntaram āha ūho vicāraś ceti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 21.2 16]
atroha ālocanajñānaṃ nirvikalpakam vicāro heyopādeyatayā vikalpanam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 21.2 17]
caturvidhaṃ hi vikalpakāraṇaṃ sāṃkhyā manyante tatra bāhyam indriyarūpam ābhyantaraṃ tu mano'haṃkāro buddhiśceti tritayam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 21.2 18]
tatrendriyāṇyālocayanti nirvikalpena gṛhṇantītyarthaḥ manastu saṃkalpayati heyopādeyatayā kalpayatītyarthaḥ ahaṃkāro 'bhimanyate mamedamahamatrādhikṛta iti manyata ityarthaḥ buddhir adhyavasyati tyajāmyenaṃ doṣavantam upādadāmyenaṃ guṇavantam ityadhyavasāyaṃ karotītyarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 21.2 19]
ūhas tu yadyapi bāhyacakṣurādikarma tathāpi tatrāpi mano'dhiṣṭhānam astīti manaḥkarmatayoktaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 21.2 20]
vacanaṃ hi sāntaḥkaraṇā buddhiḥ sarvaṃ viṣayam avagāhate yasmāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 21.2 21]
tasmāt trividhaṃ karaṇaṃ dvāri dvārāṇi śeṣāṇi iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 21.2 22]
tataḥ paraṃ buddhiḥ pravartata iti ūhavicārānantaraṃ buddhir adhyavasāyaṃ karotītyarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 21.2 23]
ahaṃkāravyāpāraś cābhimananam ihānukto 'pi buddhivyāpāreṇaiva sūcito jñeyaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 21.2 24]
buddhirhi tyajāmyenamupādadāmīti vādhyavasāyaṃ kurvatī ahaṃkārābhimata eva viṣaye bhavati tena buddhivyāpāreṇaivāhaṃkāravyāpāro 'pi gṛhyate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 21.2 25]
buddhau hi sarvakaraṇavyāpārārpaṇaṃ bhavati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 21.2 26]
yaduktam ete pradīpakalpāḥ parasparavilakṣaṇā guṇaviśeṣāḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 21.2 27]
kṛtsnaṃ puruṣasyārthaṃ prakāśya buddhau prayacchanti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 21.2 27.1]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 23.2}
etadevohavicārapūrvakatvaṃ buddher vivṛṇoti indriyeṇetyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 23.2 1]
gṛhyate iti ūhamātreṇa nirvikalpena gṛhyate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 23.2 2]
guṇata iti upādeyatayā | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 23.2 3]
doṣata iti heyatayā | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 23.2 4]
buddhyadhyavasāyaṃ vivṛṇoti jāyata ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 23.2 5]
viṣaye tatreti manasā kalpite viṣaye | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 23.2 6]
niścayātmiketi sthirasvarūpā adhyavasāyarūpetyarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 23.2 7]
vyavasyatīti anuṣṭhānaṃ karoti udyukto bhavatītyarthaḥ buddhyadhyavasitamarthaṃ vaktuṃ kartuṃ vānutiṣṭhatīti yāvat | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 23.2 8]
buddhipūrvakamityanena yadeva buddhipūrvakam anuṣṭhānaṃ tad evaivaṃvidhaṃ bhavati nonmattādyanuṣṭhānamiti darśayati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 23.2 9]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 24.2}
mano'bhidhāyendriyāṇyabhidhatte tatrāpi jyāyastvād buddhīndriyāṇi prāgāha ekaiketyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 24.2 1]
khādīnāṃ madhye ekaikenādhikena bhūtena yuktānīndriyāṇi pañca cakṣurādīni ekaikādhikapadena pañcāpi pāñcabhautikāni paraṃ cakṣuṣi tejo'dhikamityādyuktaṃ sūcayati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 24.2 2]
karmānumeyānīti kāryānumeyāni kāryaṃ cakṣurbuddhyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 24.2 3]
yebhyo buddhiḥ pravartata iti yāni buddhīndriyāṇi tānīmāni pañceti darśayati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 24.2 4]
yadyapi ca sāṃkhye āhaṃkārikāṇīndriyāṇi yaduktaṃ sāttvika ekādaśakaḥ pravartate vaikṛtād ahaṃkārād iti tathāpi matabhedādbhautikatvam indriyāṇāṃ jñeyaṃ kiṃvā aupacārikam etadbhautikatvam indriyāṇāṃ jñeyam upacārabījaṃ ca yad guṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ yad indriyaṃ gṛhṇāti tattadbhūyiṣṭham ityucyate cakṣustejo gṛhṇāti tena taijasam ucyate ityādi jñeyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 24.2 5]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 26.2}
atha karmendriyāṇyāha hastāv ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 26.2 1]
hastāv ekaṃ pādau caikamindriyamekarūpakarmakartṛtayā | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 26.2 2]
gudopasthaṃ caikaikam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 26.2 3]
vāca upādānahānārthaṃ bhedamāha vāk cetyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 26.2 4]
jyotiriva jyotiḥ dharmakartṛtvenobhayalokaprakāśakāritvāt etadviparyayeṇa tamaḥ anṛtā | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 26.2 5]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 27.2}
sampratyuddeśakramānurodhādarthe 'bhidhātavye 'rthānāṃ prakṛtigrahaṇagṛhītapañcabhūtaguṇatayā parādhīnatvād aṣṭadhātuprakṛtigṛhītāni bhūtānyeva tāvadāha mahābhūtānītyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 27.2 1]
śabdādayo yathāsaṃkhyaṃ khādīnāṃ naisargikā guṇā jñeyāḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 27.2 2]
yastu guṇotkarṣo 'bhidhātavyaḥ sa hi anupraviṣṭabhūtasambandhād eva | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 27.2 3]
tena pṛthivyāṃ caturbhūtapraveśāt pañcaguṇatvam evaṃ jalādāv api caturguṇatvādi jñeyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 27.2 4]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 28.2}
naisargikaṃ guṇamabhidhāya bhūtāntarapraveśakṛtaṃ guṇam āha teṣām ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 28.2 1]
ekaguṇaḥ pūrva iti pūrvo dhātuḥ kharūpaḥ śabdaikaguṇaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 28.2 2]
puṃliṅgatā ca khādīnāṃ dhāturūpatābuddhisthīkṛtatvāt uktaṃ hi khādayaś cetanāṣaṣṭhā dhātavaḥ iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 28.2 3]
yathā yathā ca paratvaṃ tathā tathā ca guṇavṛddhir yathāsaṃkhyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 28.2 4]
nanu etāvatā 'py ekaguṇatvadviguṇatvādi na niyamena jñāyate ko guṇaḥ kva bhūte ityāha pūrva ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 28.2 5]
guṇiṣu khādiṣu dhātuṣu pūrvo guṇaḥ krameṇa yathāsaṃkhyaṃ vartate na kevalaṃ pūrvaḥ kiṃtu pūrvasyāpi yo guṇaḥ sa ca pūrvaguṇa uttare bhūte vartate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 28.2 6]
tena khe pūrve pūrvaḥ śabdaguṇo vartate vāyau tu sparśaḥ kramaprāptaḥ pūrvo bhavati pūrvaguṇaśca śabda iti dviguṇatvam evamagnyādau ca jñeyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 28.2 7]
gandhas tūttaraguṇāntarābhāvānna pūrvo bhavati tathāpi gandhaś ca tadguṇāḥ iti granthe tadguṇā itipadāpekṣayā gandhasya pūrvatvaṃ kalpanīyaṃ kiṃvā pūrva iti chattriṇo gacchantīti nyāyenoktaṃ tenāpūrvo 'pi gandhaḥ kramāgataḥ pṛthivyāṃ jñeyaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 28.2 8]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 30.2}
bhūtānām asādhāraṇaṃ lakṣaṇamāha kharetyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 30.2 1]
apratīghātaḥ apratihananam asparśatvam iti yāvat sparśavaddhi gativighātakaṃ bhavati nākāśaḥ asparśavattvāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 30.2 2]
sarvamevaitaditi kharatvādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 30.2 3]
sparśanendriyagocaramiti sparśanendriyajñeyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 30.2 4]
kathametatsarvaṃ sparśanendriyajñeyam ityāha sparśanetyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 30.2 5]
saviparyaya iti sparśābhāva ityarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 30.2 6]
yad indriyaṃ yadgṛhṇāti tattasyābhāvamapi gṛhṇāti tena ākāśasyāsparśatvam api sparśanendriyagrāhyam iti yuktam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 30.2 7]
dravatvaṃ calatvaṃ ca sāṃkhyamate sparśanagrāhyatvāt sthūlabhūtavātadharmaḥ sparśa eva yaddhi sparśanena gṛhyate tat sarvaṃ mahābhūtavātapariṇāma eva | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 30.2 8]
etāni ca khādīni sūkṣmāṇi tanmātrarūpāṇi jñeyāni sthūlabhūtāni tu khādīni vikāratayā tatroktāni | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 30.2 9]
prakṛtivarge sūkṣmarūpāstanmātrā uktāḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 30.2 10]
vacanaṃ hi tanmātrāṇyaviśeṣās tebhyo bhūtāni pañca pañcabhyaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 30.2 11]
ete smṛtā viśeṣāḥ śāntā ghorāśca mūḍhāśca iti tenehāpi khādīni tanmātraśabdoktāni sūkṣmāṇi boddhavyāni | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 30.2 12]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 31.1}
bhūtānāṃ sūkṣmāṇāṃ śarīrasthānāṃ liṅgāntarāṇyāha guṇā ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 31.1 1]
guṇāḥ śabdādayaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 31.1 2]
guṇināmiti sūkṣmarūpabhūtānām | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 31.1 3]
evacagrahaṇāt śabdādayaśca vyaktāḥ sūkṣmāṇāṃ śarīrasthānāṃ bhūtānāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ bhavantīti vākyārthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 31.1 4]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 31.2}
arthānāha arthā ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 31.2 1]
arthaśabdena tu ye śabdādayo'bhidhīyante te sthūlakhādirūpā eva jñeyāḥ yenākāśapariṇāma eva śabdaḥ vātapariṇāmaḥ sparśa ityādi darśanam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 31.2 2]
śabdādigrahaṇaṃ nātrākāśādigrahaṇaṃ yat tadākāśādipariṇāma eva śabdādaya iti yuktameva | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 31.2 3]
etena yacchrotragrāhyaṃ tat sarvam ākāśaṃ śabdaśca yat sparśena gṛhyate tat sarvaṃ vāyuḥ sparśaścetyādi jñeyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 31.2 4]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 34.2}
saṃprati prakṛtigaṇapraviṣṭāyā buddher upadarśanārthaṃ tasyā buddhervṛttibhedāt jñānaviśeṣarūpāṇyāha yetyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 34.2 1]
yadindriyamāśrityeti yadindriyapraṇālikām āśritya mahacchabdākhyasya buddhitattvasya vṛttiviśeṣarūpāṇi jñānānīndriyapraṇālikayā bhavanti tadindriyajanyatvenaiva tāni vyapadiśyante cakṣurbuddhiḥ śrotrabuddhirityādivyapadeśena | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 34.2 2]
manobhavā ca buddhiścintyādiviṣayā manasā nirdiśyate manobuddhiriti vyapadiśyata ityarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 34.2 3]
indriyamanobhedena ṣaṭtvaṃ buddhīnāṃ pratipādya buddhibahutvaṃ prāha bhedādityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 34.2 4]
kāryasya indriyārthasya ca bhedāt tatsaṃbandhena bhidyamānā bahvyo buddhayo bhavanti kāryaṃ sukhaduḥkhabhedāḥ sukhaduḥkhaprapañcena hi tatkāryeṇa kāraṇaṃ jñānamapi bahu bhavati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 34.2 5]
idānīṃ sarvabāhyajñānasādhanamāha ātmetyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 34.2 6]
ātmā avyaktam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 34.2 7]
ekaiketi pratyekam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 34.2 8]

anena dṛṣṭāntena śabdadvayamāha aṅgulyaṅguṣṭhatalajaśabda ekaḥ ayaṃ cāṅguṣṭhayantritamadhyamāṅgulyāḥ karatalasaṃyogājjāyamānatalaśabda ucyate tantrīvīṇānakhodbhavaśca vīṇāśabda ekaḥ anye tvekam evāṅgulyādijaṃ vīṇāśabdaṃ varṇayanti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 34.2 10]
etena yathā śabdo'ṅgulādyanyatamavaikalye'pi na bhavati tathā buddhir apyātmādīnām anyatamavaikalye'pi na bhavatīti darśayati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 34.2 11]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 35.2}
atra ca buddhivṛttīnāṃ jñānānāṃ kathanenaivāhaṃkāro'pi sūcita eva yato'haṅkāropajīvitaivātmādisaṃvaliteyaṃ buddhiḥ ahaṃ paśyāmi ityādirūpā bhavati tena buddherahaṅkārasya coktatvād avaśiṣṭam avyaktaṃ kāryadvārā brūte buddhītyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 35.2 1]
paramiti avyaktam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 35.2 2]
buddhyādīnāṃ yogaṃ melakaṃ dharatīti yogadharam avyaktaṃ hi prakṛtirūpaṃ puruṣārthapravṛttaṃ buddhyādimelakaṃ bhogasaṃpādakaṃ sṛjati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 35.2 3]
evaṃ vyutpāditaṃ caturviṃśatikam upasaṃharati caturviṃśatika ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 35.2 4]
yadi vā karmendriyāṇyabhidhāya mahābhūtānītyādinā arthā evāśrayabhūtakhādikathanenocyante yā yad indriyam āśrityetyādinā tu sphuṭopalabhyamānā buddhivṛttibhedā ucyante buddhyahaṃkāratanmātrāṇyavyaktāni tu sūkṣmāṇi noktāni tāni sarvāṇyeva buddhīndriyamano'rthānām ityādigranthe paraśabdenocyante tena yogadharaṃ paramityanena mūlaprakṛtistathā prakṛtivikṛtayaśca mahadādayaḥ saptocyante evaṃ caturviṃśatiko rāśirbhavati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 35.2 5]
paratvaṃ ca vikārāpekṣayā prakṛtīnām upapannameva | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 35.2 6]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 36.2}
saṃpratyevaṃrūpapuruṣasya sakāraṇaṃ saṃsaraṇaṃ mokṣahetuṃ cāha raja ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 36.2 1]

sattvaṃ vṛddhaṃ viśuddhajñānajananād rajastamasī saṃsārakāraṇe vijitya prakṛtipuruṣavivekajñānānmokṣamāvahati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 36.2 5]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 38.2}

svatā mamatā | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 38.2 5]
jñānaṃ ca yadyapi caturviṃśatitattvātiriktasyodāsīnasyaiva tathāpi taccetanayā prakṛtirapi cetanāmāpadya cetanaiva bhavatīti yuktam atra jñānam iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 38.2 6]

yacca kiṃcanetyanenānuktamapi kṛtsnaṃ jñeyamavaruṇaddhi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 38.2 11]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 42.2}
puruṣaḥ kāraṇaṃ kasmāditi praśnasyottaraṃ bhāstama ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 42.2 1]
bhāḥ pratibhā | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 42.2 2]
tamaḥ mohaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 42.2 3]
puruṣa iha prakaraṇe ātmābhipretaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 42.2 4]
āśrayaḥ śarīram | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 42.2 5]
gatiśca prayojanānusaṃdhānād bhavati evam āgatirapi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 42.2 6]
kāraṇaṃ puruṣastasmāditi bhāstamaḥsatyādau kāraṇaṃ puruṣa ityarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 42.2 7]
etadeva bhādikāraṇatvam ātmana āha na cedityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 42.2 8]
evaṃ manyate bhāstamasī dharmādharmajanye dharmādharmau cāsatyātmani nirāśrayau na bhavitumarhataḥ tathā satyaṃ dharmajanakatayā upādeyam anṛtaṃ cādharmajanakatayānupādeyam etaccātmani sthire'sati dharmādharmajanakatvaṃ nāsti tataśca satyāsatyabhedo 'pyakiṃcitkaratvānnāsti evaṃ śubhāśubhakarmaṇyapi vācyaṃ tathā kartā ca kāraṇapratisaṃdhātā na bhavati pratisaṃdhātur ātmano 'bhāvād ityarthaḥ tathā boddhā ca pūrvāparāvasthāpratisaṃdhātaiva bhavati śarīraṃ cātmano bhogāyatanaṃ nātmānaṃ vinā bhavati evaṃ sukhādāvapyātmanaḥ kāraṇatvamunneyam vijñānaṃ śāstrārthajñānaṃ śāstrāṇi pratisaṃdhātrātmanaiva kṛtāni | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 42.2 9]
na caiṣu sambhavejjñānamiti ātmānaṃ jñātāraṃ vinā na bhādiṣu jñānaṃ sambhavet jñāturātmano'bhāvādityarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 42.2 10]
na ca taiḥ syāt prayojanam iti bhādīnām ātmārthatvenāsatyātmani bhādyutpatteḥ prayojanaṃ na syāt prayojanābhāvāccotpādo na syāt sarveṣāmeva hi bhāvānām ātmasthau dharmādharmau puruṣabhogārthamutpādakau asati bhoktari bhojyenāpi na bhavitavyaṃ kāraṇābhāvāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 42.2 11]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 44.2}

{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 47.2}

{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 49.2}

{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 51.2}

{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 58.2}
atraiva sāmagrījanyatve sarvakāryāṇāmupapattimāha na hyeka ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 58.2 1]
eko bhāvaḥ kāraṇarūpaḥ sahakārikāraṇāntararahito na kāryakaraṇe vartata ityarthaḥ evaṃ tāvadekaṃ kāraṇaṃ kārye na vartate kāryaṃ ca hetuṃ vinā na bhavatītyāha vartate nāpyahetuka iti hetuṃ vinā bhāva utpattidharmā na vartate na bhavatītyarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 58.2 2]
tena karaṇayuktātmajanyaṃ kāryaṃ na kevalādātmano heturūpād bhavatītyuktaṃ bhavati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 58.2 3]
atha hetuṃ vinā cedbhāvo na bhavati tat kimabhāve'pi śārīrāṇāṃ bhāvānāṃ hetvapekṣā na vetyāha śīghragatvādityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 58.2 4]
śīghragatvāt svabhāvāllakṣito'bhāvo na svabhāvaṃ vyativartate śīghragatvasvabhāvaṃ na tyajatītyarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 58.2 5]
tena ahetuka evābhāvo bhavati bhāvastu sahetukaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 58.2 6]
uktaṃ hi utpattihetur bhāvānāṃ na nirodhe'sti kāraṇam iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 58.2 7]
kiṃvā śīghragatvād asthiratvād abhāvo nāvasthāntaramātmanāśaṃ pratigacchatīti granthārthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 58.2 8]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 59.2}
sa nityaḥ kimanityaḥ ityasyottaramanādir ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 59.2 1]
anādiśca puruṣo'vyaktarūpa ātmaśabdābhidheyaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 59.2 2]
viparīta iti ādimān rāśirūpaḥ puruṣa ityarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 59.2 3]
atraivānāder nityatve śāstrāntarasaṃmatim apyāha sadityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 59.2 4]
sad iti trividhasamaye pramāṇagamyabhāvarūpam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 59.2 5]
etena prāgabhāvasyākāraṇavato 'pyabhāvarūpatayānityatvaṃ na vyabhicārakam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 59.2 6]
hetujamanyatheti atrāpi bhāvarūpamiti yojanīyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 59.2 7]
tena hetujanyasyāpi pradhvaṃsasyāvināśitvaṃ parihṛtaṃ bhavati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 59.2 8]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 62.2}
kiṃ tannityatvamityāha tadevetyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 62.2 1]
bhāvādutpattidharmakāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 62.2 2]
tannityatvaṃ na kuto'pi bhāvādbhavati nityaṃ hi na kuto'pi bhavati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 62.2 3]
tataścātmā bhāvaṃ prati nirapekṣatvāt sarvebhyo bhāvebhyo'pyagre nityaṃ sadeva | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 62.2 4]
taccaivaṃbhūtaṃ nityamavyaktaṃ jñeyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 62.2 5]
acintyamityavyaktaviśeṣaṇam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 62.2 6]
avyaktaṃ ca mūlaprakṛtiḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 62.2 7]
vyaktam anyatheti prakṛteranyatamakāryaṃ mahadādikamanityam ākāśamapi vikārarūpatayānityameva udāsīnapuruṣastu nitya evāvyaktaśabdenaiva lakṣita ityuktameva | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 62.2 8]
avyaktadharmāntaravyāpakān paryāyānāha avyaktam ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 62.2 9]
punaḥ prakārāntareṇa vyaktāvyaktārtham āha vakṣyata ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 62.2 10]
aparaṃ dvayamiti prakārāntarakṛtaṃ vyaktāvyaktadvayam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 62.2 11]
liṅgagrāhyamiti anumānagrāhyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 62.2 12]
atīndriyam ityanena cendriyagrahaṇāyogyaṃ yat kenāpi śabdādiliṅgena gṛhyate na tadavyaktaṃ kiṃtu yannityānumeyaṃ mano'haṅkārādi tadevāvyaktam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 62.2 13]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 64.2}
prakṛtiḥ kā vikārāḥ ke ityasyottaraṃ khādīnītyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 64.2 1]
khādīni sūkṣmabhūtakhādīni tanmātraśabdābhidheyāni | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 64.2 2]
buddhiḥ mahacchabdābhidheyā | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 64.2 3]
avyaktaṃ mūlaprakṛtiḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 64.2 4]
ahaṅkāraḥ buddhivikāraḥ sa ca trividhaḥ bhūtādiḥ taijasaḥ vaikārikaśca | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 64.2 5]
bhūtānāṃ sthāvarajaṅgamānāṃ prakṛtir bhūtaprakṛtiḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 64.2 6]
atra cāvyaktaṃ prakṛtireva paraṃ buddhyādayastu svakāraṇavikṛtirūpā api svakāryāpekṣayā prakṛtirūpā iha prakṛtitvenoktāḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 64.2 7]
yaduktaṃ mūlaprakṛtir avikṛtirmahadādyāḥ prakṛtivikṛtayaḥ sapta iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 64.2 8]
vikārānāha vikārā ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 64.2 9]
evaśabdo bhinnakrame'vadhāraṇe tena vikārā eva ṣoḍaśa paraṃ na prakṛtayaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 64.2 10]
buddher indriyāṇi buddhīndriyāṇi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 64.2 11]
pañcārthā iti sthūlā ākāśādayaḥ śabdādirūpāḥ guṇaguṇinorhi paramārthato bhedo nāstyevāsmin darśane | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 64.2 12]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 65.2}
enam eva prakṛtivikārasamūhaṃ kṣetrakṣetrajñabhedena vibhajate itītyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 65.2 1]

{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 67.1}
saṃprati mahāpralayāntaraṃ yathādisarge buddhyādyutpādo bhavati tadāha jāyata ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 67.1 1]
buddhyāhamiti manyata iti buddherjāte nāhaṅkāreṇāhamiti manyata ityarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 67.1 2]
khādīnīti khādīni sūkṣmāṇi tanmātrarūpāṇi tathaikādaśendriyāṇi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 67.1 3]
vacanaṃ hi prakṛter mahāṃstato 'haṅkārastasmād gaṇaśca ṣoḍaśakaḥ iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 67.1 4]
yathākramamiti yasmādahaṅkārādutpadyate tena krameṇa tatra vaikṛtāt sāttvikādahaṅkārāttaijasasahāyād ekādaśendriyāṇi bhavanti bhūtādestvahaṅkārāttāmasāttaijasasahāyāt pañcatanmātrāṇi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 67.1 5]
yaduktaṃ sāttvika ekādaśakaḥ pravartate vaikṛtādahaṅkārāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 67.1 6.1]
bhūtādestanmātraḥ sa tāmasastaijasādubhayam iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 67.1 6.2]
tata iti āhaṅkārikakāryānantaraṃ tanmātrebhya utpannasthūlabhūtasaṃbandhāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 67.1 7.1]
sampūrṇasarvāṅgo jāta iti ādisarge jātaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 67.1 8]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 69.2}
evamādisarge prakṛter mahadādisargaṃ darśayitvā mahāpralaye prakṛtāvavyaktarūpāyāṃ buddhyādīnāṃ layamāha puruṣa ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 69.2 1]
iṣṭair bhāvairiti puruṣopabhogārthamiṣṭair buddhyādibhiḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 69.2 2]
anye tu evaṃbhūtasaṅgaṃ janmani buddhyādiviyogaṃ ca maraṇe bruvate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 69.2 3]
tanna janmamaraṇayor buddhyādīnāṃ vidyamānatvāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 69.2 4]
uktaṃ hi atīndriyaistair atisūkṣmarūpair ātmā kadācinna vimuktapūrvaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 69.2 5.1]
naivendriyair naiva manomatibhyāṃ na cāpyahaṅkāravikāradoṣaiḥ iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 69.2 5.2]
tathānyatrāpyuktaṃ pūrvotpannam asaktaṃ niyataṃ mahadādisūkṣmaparyantam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 69.2 6.1]
saṃsarati nirupabhogaṃ bhāvairadhivāsitaṃ liṅgam iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 69.2 6.2]
tasmānmahāpralaya eva prakṛtau layaḥ tathādisarga eva prakṛtermahadādisṛṣṭiriti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 69.2 7]
etadeva prapañcaṃ layaṃ ca prakṛterāha avyaktād ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 69.2 8]
avyaktāditi prakṛteḥ vyaktatāmiti mahadādimahābhūtaparyantaprapañcarūpatāṃ yāti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 69.2 9]
avyaktād iti mahābhūtaprapañcādyavasthātaḥ punaravyaktarūpatāṃ yāti gacchati mahāpralaye hi mahābhūtāni tanmātreṣu layaṃ yānti tanmātrāṇi tathendriyāṇi cāhaṅkāre layaṃ yānti ahaṅkāro buddhau buddhiśca prakṛtāviti layakramaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 69.2 10]
ayaṃ ca layakramo mokṣe'pi bhavati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 69.2 11]
paraṃ tu tatra taṃ puruṣaṃ prati punaḥ sargaṃ nārabhate prakṛtiḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 69.2 12]
ayaṃ saṃsāraḥ kuto bhavatītyāha raja ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 69.2 13]
āviṣṭo yuktaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 69.2 14]
cakravat parivartata iti punaḥ punar layasargābhyāṃ yujyate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 69.2 15]
dvandva iti rajastamorūpe mithune | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 69.2 16]
ahaṃkāraparā iti ahaṃkārānmamedam ityādimithyājñānaparāḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 69.2 17]
udayapralayau janmamaraṇe kiṃvā layasargau | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 69.2 18]
ato'nyatheti ye rāgadveṣavimuktā nirahaṃkārāśca teṣāṃ nodayapralayau bhavataḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 69.2 19]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 74.2}
kiṃ liṅgaṃ puruṣasya ca ityasyottaraṃ prāṇāpānāvityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 74.2 1]
prāṇāpānau ucchvāsaniḥśvāsau | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 74.2 2]
nimeṣādyā iti ādyaśabdagrahaṇena unmeṣādyāḥ prekṣaṇaviśeṣā gṛhyante | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 74.2 3]
manaso gatiriti manasā pāṭaliputragamanādirūpā | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 74.2 4]
indriyāntarasaṃcāro'pi manasa eva yathā cakṣuḥ parityajya manaḥ sparśanamadhitiṣṭhatītyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 74.2 5]
preraṇaṃ ca tathā dhāraṇaṃ ca manasa eveti jñeyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 74.2 6]
deśāntaragatiḥ svapne iti chedaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 74.2 7]
pañcatvagrahaṇaṃ maraṇajñānam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 74.2 8]

cetanā jñānamātram | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 74.2 10]
buddhistu ūhāpohajñānam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 74.2 11]
atha kathametānyātmānaṃ gamayantītyāha yasmād ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 74.2 12]
jīvata iti pañcabhūtātiriktātmasaṃyuktasya | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 74.2 13]
pañcatvaṃ tu yadyapi jīvato na bhavati kiṃtu mṛtasyaiva tathāpi pañcatvaṃ mṛtaśarīre dṛśyamānaṃ viparyayāt pañcatvābhāvājjīvaccharīraliṅgaṃ bhavatīti jñeyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 74.2 14]
atraivodāhṛtāśca prāṇāpānādayo na bhūtamātre bhavanti nirātmakeṣviṣṭakāmṛtaśarīrādiṣvadarśanāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 74.2 15]

nāpīndriyāṇyātmatvena svīkartuṃ pāryante yatastathā sati indriyāntaropalabdham arthaṃ nendriyāṇi yajñadattopalabdham arthaṃ devadatta iva pratisaṃdhātuṃ samarthāni bhaveyuḥ asti cendriyāntaropalabdhārthapratisaṃdhānaṃ yathā surabhicandanaṃ spṛśāmītyatra | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 74.2 17]
tasmān mana indriyabhūtātirikta ātmā tiṣṭhatīti jñeyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 74.2 18]
atra yadyapi buddhiśabdena cetanādhṛtismṛtyahaṅkārāḥ prāpyanta eva buddhiprakāratvena tathāpi pṛthakpṛthagarthagamakatvena punaḥ pṛthagupāttāḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 74.2 19]
tathāhi cetanā guṇatvena acetanakhādibhūtātiriktadharmeṇātmānaṃ gamayati dhṛtistu niyamātmikā niyantāramātmānaṃ gamayati buddhistu ūhāpohayorekaṃ kāraṇaṃ gamayatyātmānaṃ smṛtistu pūrvānubhūtārthasmartāraṃ sthāyinamātmānaṃ gamayatītyādyanusaraṇīyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 74.2 20]
ātmādhiṣṭhānābhāve śarīre prāṇādyabhāvamāha śarīram ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 74.2 21]
śūnyāgāramiva śūnyāgāraṃ yathā adhiṣṭhātṛśūnyam evaṃ mṛtaśarīramapi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 74.2 22]
ṣaḍdhātukaṃ śarīraṃ tatra ṣaṣṭhe ātmani gate pañcabhūtātmakaṃ śarīraṃ bhavati tena pañcatvaṃ gatamucyate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 74.2 23]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 76.2}
niṣkriyasya kriyā tasya katham ityasyottaram acetanamityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 76.2 1]
cetayitā para iti para ātmā cetayitā paraṃ na tu sākṣāt kriyāvān | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 76.2 2]
nanu yadyevaṃ kathaṃ tasya kriyetyāha yuktasyetyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 76.2 3]
ātmādhiṣṭhitasyaiva manasaḥ kriyā upacārād ātmanaḥ kriyetyucyata ityarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 76.2 4]
etad evopapādayati cetanāvānityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 76.2 5]
cetanena hyātmanādhiṣṭhitaṃ manaḥ kriyāsu pravartate cetanānadhiṣṭhitaṃ tu manaḥ kriyāsu na pravartate tena yatkṛtā sā kriyā sa eva kriyāvāniti vyapadeṣṭuṃ yujyate natvacetanaṃ manaḥ tat parādhīnakriyatvena paramārthataḥ kriyāvad api kartṛtvena nocyata iti vākyārthaḥ nocyate iti kartṛ iti śeṣaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 76.2 6]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 77.2}
svatantratve 'pyaniṣṭayonigamanam ākṣiptaṃ samādadhāti yathāsvenetyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 77.2 1]
saṃprati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 77.2 1.1]
sarvāsu naragohastikīṭādiyoniṣu | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 77.2 2]
prāṇaistantrayate prāṇairyojayati ātmanaivāyaṃ dharmādharmasahāyenātmānaṃ sarvayoniṣu nayati na paraprerito yāti yato nānyaḥ puruṣo'sya prerako'sti īśvarābhāvāt kiṃvā satyapi īśvare tasyāpi karmaparādhīnatvāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 77.2 3]

{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 78.2}
vaśī yadyasukhaiḥ kasmādbhāvair ākramyate ityasyottaraṃ vaśītyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 78.2 1]
vaśī svecchādhīnapravṛttiḥ iṣṭe'niṣṭe vātmā tena vaśī sannayaṃ tāni karmāṇi karoti śubhānyaśubhāni vā āpātaphalarāgāt yāni kṛtvā tatkarmaprabhāvācchubhenāśubhena vā phalena yogamāpnoti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 78.2 2]
etena kartavye karmaṇyasya vaśitvaṃ kṛtakarmaphalaṃ tv asyānicchato 'pi bhavati tena tatprati nāsya vaśitvam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 78.2 3]
anyadapi vaśitvaphalamāha vaśī cetaḥ samādhatta iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 78.2 4]
aniṣṭe'rthe vaśī sannayaṃ mano nivartayati yadi hyayaṃ vaśī na syāt na mano nivartayituṃ śaknuyāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 78.2 5]
aparamapi vaśitvagamakaṃ karmāha vaśī sarvaṃ nirasyatīti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 78.2 6]
vaśī sannayaṃ mokṣārthaṃ pravṛttaḥ sarvārambhaṃ śubhāśubhaphalaṃ tyajatītyarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 78.2 7]
iha svatantraḥ parātmanā īśvarādinā preritapravṛttir ucyate vaśī tu svayamapi pravartamāna icchāvaśāt pravartate na preritapravṛttirūpatvenepsite'nīpsite ca vartate iti svātantryavaśitvayorbhedaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 78.2 8]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 79.2}
sarvāḥ sarvagatatvācca vedanāḥ kiṃ na vetti saḥ ityasyottaramāha dehītyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 79.2 1]
sarvagata iti sarvagato'pi san saṃsparśanendriya iti saṃsparśanayukte śarīre vedanāḥ sukhaduḥkharūpā vetti sarvāśrayasthāstu na vettīti yojanā | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 79.2 2]
yasmāt sarvagato'pyātmā svakīya eva sparśanavati śarīre paraṃ vedanā vetti tena sarvāśrayasthāḥ sarvavedanā na vettīti vākyārthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 79.2 3]
sarvāśrayasthā iti sarvaparaśarīragatāḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 79.2 4]
paraśarīre cātmā svakarmopārjitendriyābhāvād vidyamāno'pi nopalabhate sukhaduḥkhe | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 79.2 5]
sve sve śarīra iti vaktavye yatra saṃsparśanendriye iti karoti tena svaśarīre'pi yatra keśanakhādau sparśanendriyaṃ nāsti tatra nātmā kiṃcidupalabhata iti darśayati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 79.2 6]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 81.2}
na paśyati vibhuḥ kasmāt ityādipraśnasyottaraṃ vaktuṃ pravṛtto vibhutvasādhakārthaguṇahetuprāptyā vibhutvam eva tāvadātmanaḥ sādhayati vibhutvam ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 81.2 1]
vibhutvaṃ sarvagataparimāṇayogitvam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 81.2 2]
ata eveti uktasarvagatatvāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 81.2 3]
etadeva spaṣṭārthaṃ sākṣād brūte yasmād ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 81.2 4]
sarvagatatvaṃ sarvato'pyupalabhyamānatvena sarvagatākāśādiparimāṇasyāpyasti tena tadvyavacchedārthaṃ mahān iti padaṃ tena sarvatropalabhyamānaṃ mahāparimāṇayogidravyaṃ vibhurucyata iti phalati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 81.2 5]
vibhutvaṃ vyutpādya kuḍyatirohitajñānaṃ naikāntena bhavatīti darśayannāha manasa ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 81.2 6]
samādhānaṃ samādhiḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 81.2 7]
anena yoginaḥ samādhibalāt tirohitamapi paśyatīti darśayati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 81.2 8]
ye tu tirohitaṃ na paśyanti tatrāpyupapattimāha nityetyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 81.2 9]
sarvayonigatamapyātmānaṃ manasānubandhagatam ekayonāvavasthitaṃ vidyād iti yojyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 81.2 10]
dehanirvartakena karmaṇā anupāta ātmani saṃbandho yasya tena manasā dehakarmānupātinā | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 81.2 11]
etena yadyapyātmā kuḍyādibhir atirohitas tathāpi yad asyopalabdhisādhanaṃ manastasyaikasminneva śarīre vyavasthitasya vyavadhānānna paśyatyayaṃ tiraskṛtam ityuktaṃ bhavati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 81.2 12]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 82.2}
kṣetrajñaḥ kṣetramathavā ityādipraśnasyottaram ādir ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 82.2 1]
kṣetrapāraṃparyamiti kṣetrasyāvyaktavarjitasya mahadāditrayoviṃśatikasya paramparasaṃtater anāditvenaiva kṣetrakṣetrajñayor idaṃ prathamamiti vyapadeśo naiva bhavatītyarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 82.2 2]
nanu yadi kṣetraparaṃparāpyanādis tadā tasyātmavad ucchedo na prāpnoti yadanādi tannityaṃ bhavati yathātmeti dṛṣṭaṃ brūmaḥ anāditve'pi yat svarūpenaivānādi tannocchidyate yathātmā yattu ucchittidharmakaṃ buddhyādi taducchidyata eva saṃtānastu paramārthataḥ saṃtānibhyo 'tirikto nāstyeva yadanādiḥ syāt tena saṃtānasyānāditvaṃ bhāktameva | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 82.2 3]
kiṃcaivaṃbhūtasya buddhyādisaṃtānasyocchede mokṣapratipādaka āgama eva pramāṇatvena jñeyaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 82.2 4]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 83.2}

{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 85.2}

avikārasya paramātmano vedanākṛto viśeṣo nāstyeva yatra tu vedanākṛto viśeṣaḥ sa rāśirūpaḥ paramātmavyatirikta eveti vākyārthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 85.2 2]
bhūtānāmadhiṣṭhātā ātmā bhūtātmā ayaṃ bhūtātmā eko bhūtavyatirikto na lakṣaṇaiḥ prāṇāpānādibhiruktair upalabhyate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 85.2 3]
kuto nopalabhyata ityāha viśeṣa ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 85.2 4]

saṃyogapuruṣaḥ caturviṃśatikaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 85.2 6]
nanvevamapi caturviṃśatyantarniviṣṭasya bhūtātmano'pi vedanākṛtaviśeṣeṇa bhavitavyaṃ yataḥ samudāyadharmaḥ samudāyināmeva bhavati yathā māṣarāśer gurutvaṃ pratyekaṃ māṣāṇāmeva gauraveṇa bhavatītyāha vedanetyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 85.2 7]
vedanā sukhaduḥkharūpā | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 85.2 8]
yatra buddhyādisamūhe niyatā vyavasthitā vedanā tatraiva tatkṛto dainyaharṣādiviśeṣo'pi niyataḥ tatraiva buddhyādirāśau vartate nātmanīti bhāvaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 85.2 9]
buddhyādigatena guṇatrayapariṇāmarūpeṇa sukhaduḥkhādinā asukhaduḥkha evātmā tatsaṃbandhāt sukhaduḥkhādimān bhavati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 85.2 10]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 94.2}
athavārtasya ityādipraśnasyottaramāha cikitsatītyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 94.2 1]

uktaṃ hi prāk saṃtāpāt api cainaṃ saṃtāpārtam anubadhnanti ityanena rogāvasthāyām api pūrvarūpasadbhāvaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 94.2 8]

pāramparyānubandhaḥ saṃtānanyāyenānubandhaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 94.2 11]
duḥkhānāmiti rogāṇām | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 94.2 12]
sukhahetūpacāreṇeti ārogyahetucikitsāsevayā | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 94.2 13]
sukhamiti ārogyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 94.2 14]
evaṃ manyate yadā cikitsā sukhahetuḥ sevyate tadā duḥkhahetusevābhāvād duḥkhaṃ notpadyate utpannaṃ ca duḥkhaṃ rogarūpaṃ kṣaṇabhaṅgitvena svayameva naśyati sukhahetusānnidhyāt sukham ārogyam utpadyate tena cikitsayā anāgataṃ duḥkhaṃ hetupratibandhānnirudhyate sukhaṃ ca janyate iti siddhāntaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 94.2 15]
etadevāha na samā ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 94.2 16]

hetubhiḥ sadṛśā iti samahetoḥ samāḥ tathā viṣamahetośca viṣamāḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 94.2 18]
etaccikitsāprābhṛtīye'dhyāye prapañcitam eva | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 94.2 19]

niṣṭhā atyantaduḥkhamokṣo mokṣarūpaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 94.2 21]

{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 97.2}
paro hetur iti mūlakāraṇam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 97.2 1]

{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 98.2}

{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 99.2}

{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 112.2}

tattvasmṛtiḥ ātmādīnāṃ yathā bhūtānusmaraṇaṃ sā ca nātmā śarīrādyupakāryaḥ śarīrādayaścāmī ātmavyatiriktāḥ ityādismaraṇarūpasmṛtiḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 146.2 10]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 147.2}
atha smṛtiḥ kathaṃ duḥkhapramoṣe kāraṇamityāha smṛtvetyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 147.2 1]
svabhāvamiti pratyātmaniyatarūpam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 147.2 2]
guruvacanāddhi prathamapratipannam ātmādīnāṃ rūpaṃ parasparabhinnaṃ parasparānupakārakatvena vyavasthitaṃ smaran na kvacidapi pravartate apravartamānaśca na duḥkhena pravṛttijanyena yujyata ityarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 147.2 3]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 149.2}
idānīṃ smṛtiprastāvāt smṛtikāraṇānyāha vakṣyanta ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 149.2 1]

rūpagrahaṇam ākāragrahaṇam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 149.2 3]
yathā vane gavayaṃ dṛṣṭvā gāṃ smarati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 149.2 4]

saviparyayāditi atyarthavaisādṛśyādapi smaraṇaṃ bhavati yathā atyarthakurūpaṃ dṛṣṭvā pratiyoginamatyarthasurūpaṃ smarati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 149.2 6]

{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 151.2}
evaṃ smṛtiṃ sāmānyena pratipādya tattvasmṛter mokṣasādhakatvaṃ darśayannāha etadityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 151.2 1]

{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 153.2}

jñaḥ tattvasākṣātkāravān | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 153.2 12]

{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 154.2}
caramasaṃnyāsa iti paścādbhāvisakalakarmasaṃnyāse | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 154.2 1]
prathamaṃ hi mokṣopayogitvena guruvacanāt kriyāsaṃnyāsaḥ kṛta eva paraṃ svānubhavaviraktena na kṛtaḥ abhyāsād udbhūtena jñānena sākṣāddṛṣṭaṃ bhāvasvabhāvena yaḥ sarvasaṃnyāsaḥ kriyate tatra samūlāḥ sarvavedanā jñānādayaśca śarīroparamādevoparamante | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 154.2 2]

{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 155.3}
sarvavid ityādipraśnasyottaram ataḥ paramityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 155.3 1]
brahmabhūta iti prakṛtyādirahitaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 155.3 2]
cihnaṃ yasya na vidyate ityanena muktātmanaḥ prāṇāpānādyātmaliṅgābhāvād gamakaṃ cihnaṃ nāstyeveti darśayati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 1, 155.3 3]

{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Śār., 2, 2}

{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Indr., 1, 7.6}
nimittānurūpeti nimittasadṛśī | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Indr., 1, 7.6 1]

aparamapi nimittānurūpāyā vikṛter viśeṣamāha tāmityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Indr., 1, 7.6 5]
animittāmiti tadātve'nupalabhyamānanimittāṃ na tu punaḥ sarvathaivāhetukīṃ yata āyuṣaḥ kṣayanimittām ityanantaramasya viśeṣaṇaṃ kathayiṣyati riṣṭasya hi na raukṣyādinā śarīrasaṃbandhādi nimittam upalabhyate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Indr., 1, 7.6 6]

atra gatāyuṣṭvameva sakalapuruṣasaṃśritariṣṭavyāpakaṃ kāraṇaṃ sādhu | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Indr., 1, 7.6 8]
yattu vakṣyati kriyāpathamatikrāntāḥ kevalaṃ dehamāśritāḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Indr., 1, 7.6 9]
cihnaṃ kurvanti yaddoṣās tadariṣṭaṃ pracakṣate iti taddūtādigatariṣṭāvyāpakatayā puruṣāśrayiriṣṭamātrābhiprāyeṇa jñeyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Indr., 1, 7.6 10]

bhūya iti atyartham | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Indr., 1, 7.6 12]

yāmiti kṣīṇāyuḥkāryām | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Indr., 1, 7.6 14]
pretaliṅgānurūpām iti pretasadṛśīṃ malā danteṣu jāyante pretākṛtir udīryate ityādigranthavakṣyamāṇām | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Indr., 1, 7.6 15]

yā tvanyā pretaliṅgānanurūpā varṇāśrayā sā pratyāsannamaraṇabodhikā tena sā nātyarthaṃ nātyarthakṣīṇāyuḥkāryetyarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Indr., 1, 7.6 17]
evaṃ bhūyaśca ityādinā dhīrāḥ ityantena nimittānurūpavikṛtiviśeṣasya kāryaviśeṣaṃ maraṇalakṣaṇam abhidhāya punaḥ sāmānyenānimittāyā dharmāntaramāha yām adhikṛtyetyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Indr., 1, 7.6 18]

yato dūtādhikārādau yāni riṣṭāni tāni dṛśyamānanimittāny apy āgamādeva riṣṭatvenāvadhāryante | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Indr., 1, 7.6 20]
yathā muktakeśe 'thavā nagne rudatyaprayate'thavā | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Indr., 1, 7.6 21.1]
bhiṣagabhyāgataṃ dṛṣṭvā dūtaṃ maraṇamādiśet | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Indr., 1, 7.6 21.2]
iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Indr., 1, 7.6 21.3]
atra ca bhiṣajo muktakeśavacanād dṛśyata eva kāraṇaṃ tathā dūtāgamane cāturasya preraṇādi kāraṇamastyeva tenānimittatvam āturāśrayiriṣṭa eva | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Indr., 1, 7.6 22]
anye tu evaṃbhūtavaidyadūtasamāgamaḥ parihartavyatvena jñātaḥ san yadā daivādbhavati tadā daivanimittaḥ san riṣṭaṃ bhavati tena sarvariṣṭavyāpikaiveyam animittatā bhūyaścetyādigranthena tu pretaliṅgānurūpāṃ vikṛtiṃ bhūya āyuṣo'ntargatasya jñānārtham upadiśanti tathā puruṣasaṃśrayāṇi bhūya upadekṣyante puruṣā nāśrayāṇi tu svalpagranthenopadekṣyante iti vyākhyānayanti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Indr., 1, 7.6 23]

anye tv atra suśrute arśaścikitsitoktaśataparyantaṃ bhallātakaprayogeṇa samaṃ virodhaṃ paśyantaḥ suśrutaprayogasyāpyanyathā vyākhyānena triṃśatkamātraṃ prayogamicchanti tacca vyākhyānaṃ nātisaṃgatam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Cik., 2, 13.6 7]
kiṃca sahasradvayasya tatropayogo vihitaḥ atra sahasraparyantaḥ prayogaḥ tena vyādhiviṣayo'nya eva sa prayogaḥ ayaṃ tu rasāyanaviṣayaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Cik., 2, 13.6 8.2]
{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Cik., 2, 14}

{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Cik., 2, 16}
bhallātakasarpir ityādayo daśaprayogāḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Cik., 2, 16 1]
atra ca yathāyogyatayā bhallātakena sarpirādīnāṃ saṃskāraḥ saṃyogaśca jñeyaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Cik., 2, 16 2]
yaduktaṃ jatūkarṇe bhallātakasaṃyuktasaṃskṛtāni ca ghṛtakṣīrakṣaudraguḍayūṣatailapalalasaktulavaṇatarpaṇāni iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Cik., 2, 16 3]
evaṃ ca sarpiḥkṣīrayūṣatailānāṃ saṃskāro yathānyāyaṃ bhallātakena kṣaudrapalalasaktutarpaṇānāṃ bhallātakena yogaḥ guḍalavaṇayostu saṃskāraḥ saṃyogo vā | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Cik., 2, 16 4]
lavaṇe saṃskārapakṣe hi lavaṇasamaṃ bhallātakam antardhūmadagdhaṃ grāhyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Cik., 2, 16 5]
anye tu sarpirādīnāṃ sarveṣāmeva bhallātakena saṃskāraṃ vyākhyānayanti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Cik., 2, 16 6]
iha saktuprayogo'dravottaratvād aviśeṣakarmaṇā bhedanīyaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Cik., 2, 16 7]

{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Cik., 22, 3.2}

cikitsitaṃ cikitsāvidhāyako granthaḥ nidānādyabhidhānaṃ ca cikitsārthameva nidānādijñānapūrvakatvāc cikitsāyāḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Cik., 22, 3.2 2]

{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Cik., 22, 7.2}

yā hi mānasī tṛṣṇā sā śarīre icchādveṣātmikā tṛṣṇā sukhaduḥkhāt pravartate ityādāv uktā iyaṃ tu dehāśrayadoṣakāraṇā satī dehajaiveti bhāvaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Cik., 22, 7.2 7]

maivaṃ tasyā ucitadravapānenaivābhipretena praśamād iha asvābhāvikavyādhiprakaraṇe nādhikāra iti hṛdi kṛtvā | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Cik., 22, 7.2 9]
svābhāvikatṛṣṇākaravātapittābhyāṃ vakṣyamāṇatṛṣṇārambhakavātapittayor viśeṣamāha pītaṃ pītam ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Cik., 22, 7.2 10]

{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Cik., 22, 8.2}
tṛṣṇāprāgrūpam āha prāgrūpam ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Cik., 22, 8.2 1]
prāgrūpakathane eva madhye tṛṣṇānāmavyabhicārilakṣaṇam āha svalakṣaṇam ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Cik., 22, 8.2 2]
svalakṣaṇam iti avyabhicārilakṣaṇaṃ yathā jvarasya saṃtāpaḥ śvayathor utsedhaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Cik., 22, 8.2 3]
punaḥ prakṛtaṃ prāgrūpam āha liṅgānāṃ lāghavamapāya iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Cik., 22, 8.2 4]
liṅgānāṃ vakṣyamāṇavātādijatṛṣṇāliṅgānāṃ lāghavam alpatvaṃ keṣāṃcic cābhāvaḥ pūrvarūpaṃ tṛṣṇānām ityarthaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Cik., 22, 8.2 5]
tena pūrvarūpāvasthāyāṃ vakṣyamāṇalakṣaṇāni kānicin na bhavantyeva yāni ca bhavanti tānyalpatayāsphuṭāni bhavanti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Cik., 22, 8.2 6]
uktaṃ ca avyaktaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ tasya pūrvarūpam iti smṛtam iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Cik., 22, 8.2 7]
kiṃvā yadetat prāgrūpaṃ mukhaśoṣaḥ svalakṣaṇaṃ sarvadāmbukāmitvam etat prāgrūpaṃ svalakṣaṇaṃ ca tṛṣṇānāṃ tena mukhaśoṣāmbukāmitve svalakṣaṇe tathā pūrvarūpe ca bhavataḥ pūrvarūpāvasthāyāṃ tv aprabale mukhaśoṣāmbukāmitve jñeye | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Cik., 22, 8.2 8]
ye tu prāgrūpaṃ mukhaśoṣaḥ svarakṣayaḥ sarvadāmbukāmitvam iti paṭhanti teṣāṃ mate tṛṣṇāyāḥ svalakṣaṇaṃ noktaṃ syāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Cik., 22, 8.2 9]
uktaṃ ca hārīte'pi tṛṣṇāsvalakṣaṇaṃ svalakṣaṇaṃ tu tṛṣṇānāṃ sarvadāmbupipāsitā iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Cik., 22, 8.2 10]
kiṃvā mukhaśoṣasvarakṣaye eva pūrvarūpaṃ sarvadāmbukāmitvaṃ ca svalakṣaṇaṃ liṅgānāṃ ca lāghavaṃ rogarūpāyās tṛṣṇāyā apāyo gamanamityarthaḥ ayameva tṛṣṇāvyuparamo yad vakṣyamāṇaliṅgānām alpatvaṃ sarvathocchedo hi tṛṣṇālakṣaṇānāṃ na bhavatyeva sahajatṛṣṇāgrastatvenaitallakṣaṇānām alpamātratayāvasthānāt | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Cik., 22, 8.2 11]
kaiścit tu liṅgānāṃ lāghavam āśūtpādaḥ sa ca apāyo maraṇam iti kṛtvā tṛṣṇānāmasādhyatālakṣaṇamidamucyate tannātimanoharam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Cik., 22, 8.2 12]

{ĀVDīp zu Ca, Si., 12, 41.1}
etacchāstrasaṃskāropapattyupadarśanapūrvakaṃ śāstrasya saṃskārakau carakadṛḍhabalau darśayannāha dṛḍhabalaḥ vistārayatītyādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Si., 12, 41.1 1]
yasmācchāstre prathamamativistāratayā kvacilleśoktyā ca pratipāditeṣu na samyagarthāvagamaḥ tena tadativistaraleśoktadoṣanirāsārthaṃ saṃskartā yujyate ataḥ tantrottamam idaṃ carakeṇa saṃskṛtam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Si., 12, 41.1 2]
pūrvagranthasya cātīva vistaratvādinā tantrābhidhānaṃ pūrvaśrotṛjanābhiprāyādeva boddhavyam idānīṃtanaśrotṛpuruṣābhiprāyeṇa tu saṃskartuḥ saṃskāro jñeyaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Si., 12, 41.1 3]
uktaṃ ca saṃkṣepoktam atihanti vistaroktaṃ na gṛhyate | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Si., 12, 41.1 4.1]
saṃkṣepavistarau hitvā saṃskuryācchāstram āditaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Si., 12, 41.1 4.2]
iti | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Si., 12, 41.1 4.3]
purāṇaṃ ca punarnavam iti vistārasaṃkṣepādinā punarnavaṃ kurute | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Si., 12, 41.1 5]
carakasaṃskārāpūrṇatāṃ darśayan dṛḍhabala āha tattvityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Si., 12, 41.1 6]
tṛtīyo bhāgastribhāgaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Si., 12, 41.1 7]
tribhāgāsaṃpūrṇatā ceyam adūrāntaratayoktā tena dṛḍhabalapratipāditaikacatvāriṃśadadhyāyānāṃ na saviṃśādhyāyaśatatribhāgatā yujyate iti nodbhāvanīyam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Si., 12, 41.1 8]
ātmanaḥ pañcanadapurabhavatvena śreṣṭhapradeśabhavatvaṃ darśayati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Si., 12, 41.1 9]
ātmanaḥ saṃskāre tantrāntarānītārthena saṃskāraṃ darśayannāha kṛtvā bahubhya ityādi | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Si., 12, 41.1 10]
tantrebhyaḥ suśrutavidehāditantrebhyaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Si., 12, 41.1 11]
viśeṣasya carakoktārthād atiriktarūpasya uñchaśilarūpa uccayo viśeṣoñchaśiloccayaḥ tamanyatantrebhyaḥ kṛtvā saptadaśauṣadhādhyāyasiddhikalpair idam anyūnaśabdārthaṃ tantradoṣavivarjitaṃ ṣaḍviṃśattantrayuktibhir bhūṣitam apūrayad dṛḍhabala iti yojanā | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Si., 12, 41.1 12]
tatra bhūmipatitānām aṇūnāṃ dhānyādibījānāṃ śodhanyā saṃharaṇam uñchaḥ praviralasya tu kaṇiśādirūpatayā patitasya cayanaṃ śilaḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Si., 12, 41.1 13]
etena tantreṣu yatsārabhūtaṃ taccarakācāryaiḥ saṃgṛhītaṃ mayā tu urvaritaṃ pariśiṣṭaṃ kṛtvā pūritam iti darśayati | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Si., 12, 41.1 14]
anyūnaśabdam anyūnārthaṃ ceti anyūnaśabdārtham | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Si., 12, 41.1 15]
tantradoṣāścaturdaśa punaruktaṃ duṣpraṇītasūtrasaṃgraham akramaṃ ityādinā rogabhiṣagjitīyoktās tair varjitam | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Si., 12, 41.1 16]
tantrayuktibhir iti vakṣyamāṇatantrayuktibhiḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Si., 12, 41.1 17]
vicitrābhiriti vicitrārthanyāyayuktābhis tantrayuktibhiḥ | [ĀVDīp zu Ca, Si., 12, 41.1 18]
